500,000 People Gather in Nuremberg, Germany for the Opening of the National Socialist Party Congress 52

Hitler Delivers Declaration

Revolution Ends, Construction Begins

Strive for Friendship and Peace with Foreign Countries

Nuremberg: The National Socialist Party Congress opened here today. Hitler read a document stating that last year the National Socialist Party's power had reached a solid position, and this year is the period for the National Socialist Party's major construction work. He had to explain that the revolution of the National Socialist Party had fully realized its expectations, because fanatics in the revolution still wanted to expand the scope of possible achievements or deliberately ignored this scope. It must be known that the revolution cannot continue forever, because endless revolutions will lead to great chaos and destroy all economic life in the country. The revolution itself is only secondary, and the most important thing is the purpose of the revolution. The current system must be replaced by a better one. The leaders of the National Socialist movement are the complete masters of Germany, and no one can deny this. The representatives of the National Socialist Party are, of course, the best people in the party in terms of intelligence and creativity. Hitler concluded that National Socialism is a world philosophy. (Fifth-day Reuters telegram)

Nuremberg: Hitler delivered a declaration at the Sixth National Socialist Party Congress, which was read by Wagner, the leader of the National Socialist Party in the Bavarian region. The second paragraph of his declaration was a statement of foreign policy, stating that Germany has no grievances and no desire for revenge. What Germany seeks is to live in peace and friendship with its enemies of fifteen years ago. If a second World War were to break out, it would inevitably plunge Europe into communist chaos. The Third Reich, in view of this, is doing everything possible to improve its external relations. However, Germany's call for peace has not been fully understood by the world, but we still do not give up this hope. Our call will eventually be understood by the world. Germany will use all means to defend its honor, independence, and freedom. Germany will never give up the rights of a great power. The reason why Germany withdrew from the League of Nations is that the League of Nations was unwilling to recognize Germany's equal rights. Finally, he reiterated Germany's domestic affairs, saying that the success of Germany's judicial reform in terms of society is unparalleled. In addition, he also mentioned Germany's industrial recovery plan and road construction plan, saying that although German exports have encountered various difficulties, the price of the Mark must be kept stable. (Fifth-day Havas telegram)

Nuremberg: The National Socialist Party's annual meeting officially opened at 11:00 AM today. Hess, the representative of the leader of the National Socialist Party, delivered the opening speech, followed by Wagner, the Minister of the Interior, reading Hitler's official instructions. The city, which is quite medieval in style, has been newly decorated everywhere today. The attendees are bustling about, making it very lively. The conference will continue tomorrow afternoon, and Propaganda Minister Goebbels will deliver an important speech. Hitler himself is scheduled to speak next Monday. Foreign guests, including the Chinese inspection team and the American newspaper tycoon Hearst, were invited by Hitler to attend. (Fifth-day National News telegram)

Nuremberg: The Sixth National Socialist Party Congress is scheduled to open here tomorrow. Members of the party in uniforms from all over Germany gathered here today, numbering about 500,000. Large swastika flags were hung in public and private houses. Thousands of tents and other temporary buildings were prepared to accommodate the party members. During the conference, seven speeches will be broadcast by radio. German leader Hitler arrived here by plane this afternoon and officially visited the medieval city hall in the evening. At the time, the church bells rang, the army drums beat, and the band played music. Tens of thousands of spectators in the square in front of the hall cheered loudly, deafeningly. Saar Issue

Memorandum from France to the League of Nations Regarding the Saar 54

If the plebiscite next year results in a return to Germany, an arbitration court should be established to protect the rights of the people, and Germany should redeem the currency and mineral resources at a fair price.

(Paris) The French memorandum to the Council of the League of Nations regarding the Saar problem has been published. Its content concerns the various measures to be taken after the Saar plebiscite. According to the Treaty of Versailles, the Saar region will be administered by the Administrative Commission of the League of Nations for fifteen years, after which it can either maintain its original status and continue to be managed by the League of Nations, be ceded to France, or be returned to Germany, all of which will be decided by a plebiscite. This French memorandum considers the three possible scenarios separately: (1) If the plebiscite is to maintain the status quo, the French government believes that the people of the Saar should participate in the discussion on how the future system of the Saar region should be organized. (2) If the result of the vote is to cede the Saar region to France, the French government is prepared to announce that under French rule, the people of the Saar will enjoy the same rights as the French people, without discrimination based on race, religion, or language. (3) If it is decided to return the Saar region to Germany, the League of Nations should take the necessary measures to protect the vested rights of the people of the Saar in terms of social insurance and pensions, legally and administratively. The German government can only redeem the francs circulating in the Saar region at a fair price for the purpose of repaying foreign debts, and cannot regard them as German

Page 10

property. As for the mineral resources operated by the French government in the Saar region, if the Saar region is returned to Germany, Germany should redeem them from France at a fair price. If the status quo is maintained, there will be no legal problem. However, the French government is well aware that mineral resources are the key to the entire economy of the Saar region. If they continue to be operated by France, it may not be compatible with the new organization after the Saar plebiscite. Therefore, it is prepared to cede most of the mineral resources to the Saar region under fair conditions. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(Paris) French Foreign Minister Barthou submitted a memorandum to the League of Nations, proposing that if the result of the plebiscite in the Saar region next year is to return the Saar region to Germany, an arbitration court of mixed nationality should be established. The French government makes this proposal because it believes that in order to ensure the safety of voters and protect the rights of residents regarding property and monetary contracts, more thorough measures must be taken. The memorandum also suggests that in order to avoid long-term delays, France and Germany should agree on a draft agreement regarding the price of Saar minerals, so that when the plebiscite approves the return of the Saar region to Germany, Germany must pay the price of the minerals to France according to this draft agreement. The price of the minerals must be paid in cash before the mineral resources can be accepted. If the result of the vote is to maintain the status quo, France is willing to hand over most of the mineral resources to the Saar local authorities under appropriate conditions. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

U.S. Textile Industry Strike Situation Worsens 57

If it Extends Beyond January

The U.S. Market Will Be Seized by Japan

(Washington) About half of the national textile industry is participating in the strike. If the strike extends beyond January, there is a risk that part of the U.S. textile industry's market will be seized by Japan. Sloan, president of the American Cotton Manufacturers Association, said in New York today that there would not be a shortage of goods for the time being, because the factories have enough inventory to meet the usual demand for four weeks. However, if the strike extends beyond four weeks, Japanese exporters can take part of the U.S. market and replace them. According to an Associated Press survey, about 50% are participating in the strike, with Connecticut being the most consistent, accounting for about 80%. There are 100,000 strikers in Pennsylvania, and 60,000 are still working as usual. In North and South Carolina, there are 750 textile factories, and only 225 are on strike. In general, there are more cotton mills than other factories, and silk mills have not responded at all. According to the leader of the United Textile Workers of America, the strike has been very successful. However, yesterday he said that 600,000 people participated, but today it has been reduced to 300,000. Judging from reports from all parties, the number of strikers is far less than the union claims. (National Telegraph, 4th)

(New York) The textile industry strike involves 1.25 million people, but there are actually many people working as usual, so those who have gone on strike are quite resentful, and there are fears of riots and bloodshed. Although today's report shows a large increase in the number of strikers, the estimate is still less than half of the total. Pickets appeared in New England and the Southern cotton region today, but they were peaceful. There have been a few minor conflicts between strikers and factory police. Governor Lehman of New York State said today that the government cannot provide relief to those who are not currently working, and that requests for relief must be studied separately. The strikers were discouraged by this statement. It is estimated that there are 50,000 strikers and 75,000 non-strikers in New England. In North and South Carolina, the number of strikers and non-strikers are about equal, at 80,000 each. 10,000 workers in the St. Louis cotton clothing industry and 5,000 in Kansas City have all received strike notices. Gorman, chairman of the strike committee, said today that he was very pleased that the textile workers obeyed orders and went on strike enthusiastically. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

11,000 People Take Direct Action

Daily Losses Estimated at 100,000 Yuan

(Tokyo) 11,000 municipal streetcar and tram employees went on strike this morning, and traffic was half-paralyzed, but some vehicles were still running in the city, driven by 600 municipal electric power department clerks and 750 other employees. No disturbances have occurred so far. It is expected that the government will submit the wage dispute to arbitration. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

(Tokyo) Negotiations between Tokyo Municipal Tram labor and management broke down. The union issued a strike order on the evening of the 4th, and all employees went on a general strike at 4:30 a.m. on the 5th. Temporary employees of the authorities drove the trams, and buses also ran temporarily. The Metropolitan Police Department dispatched a large number of police officers for serious security. The atmosphere is still calm. The Tokyo Tram Employees' General Strike reserve fund has reached tens of thousands of yuan. Each employee lives in his dormitory to maintain order. The municipal authorities temporarily recruited 2,000 employees to drive trams. In this era of unemployment, the news that 2,000 employees were recruited spread, and the city's unemployed army rushed to the Electric Power Bureau. Drivers and ticket sellers in Japanese and Western clothes immediately took up their duties. At this time, most of the temporary employees had no experience. They did not stop where they should, and stopped where they should not. The ticket sellers did not know the names of the stations. A triple collision of trams occurred near Manseibashi, causing passengers to realize the danger to their lives. This was the situation on the first day of the strike. (Japan United Press dispatch, 5th)

(Tokyo) The Tokyo Municipal Electric Company took decisive measures against the striking workers and dismissed 45 strike leaders today. The solidarity of the strike group is very strong and will not be greatly affected. The Metropolitan Police Department is observing the situation. (Japan United Press dispatch, 5th)

(Tokyo) The Tokyo Municipal Electric Company's streetcars usually carry 800,000 passengers, and its income reaches more than 51,000 yuan. The buses carry 160,000 passengers and can collect 11,000 yuan per day. This time, due to the dispute, the fare is temporarily set at 5 cents across the board. The number of vehicles has also been reduced, and its income must also be reduced by one-third. It also needs to spend various huge defense costs. After calculation, it will lose 100,000 yuan per day. (Japan United Press dispatch, 5th)

Italy Boycotts Japanese Goods 59

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Believes It Violates the Treaty

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a telegram from Iwate, the acting ambassador to Italy, on the 5th, stating that the Italian government had sent a letter to the embassy, stating that based on the reasons stated in the letter, it had decided on the 2nd to implement a distribution import system for Japanese goods such as eyeglasses, celluloid toys, and combs by order. The notice was received on the 4th. Although the eyeglasses item did not specify a distribution fee, it was explained that if Japan requested it, it would be considered in good faith. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believed that this measure by the Italian government violated the most-favored-nation treatment recognized by the treaty, that is, the absolute treatment stipulated in Article 9 of the Japan-Italy Treaty of Commerce regarding the prohibition of import and restriction of import should be eliminated. Therefore, the implementation of the above-mentioned distribution system for Japanese goods this time is recognized as a clear violation of the treaty. The letter notified by the Italian government also clearly stated that the Italian government, in view of the importance of Japanese goods imports, agreed to deal fairly with them in the past, and then implemented the distribution system, which is quite unreasonable. It has now telegraphed Iwate, the acting ambassador to Italy, to demand an explanation from the Italian government based on reason. (Japan United Press dispatch, 5th)

Sarcoma Is Caused by Microbes 90

Not Caused by Toxins

Research by German Medical Scientists

(Berlin) The discovery of tumor bacteria by Dr. Bremer, director of the Dahlem Biological Research Institute near Berlin, Germany, has been reported in various newspapers, but the details are unclear and a restatement is necessary. Dr. Bremer's report was completed two years ago. The reason for the delay in publishing it was that Dr. Bremer's experimental results had to be reviewed by several well-known German experts, which took a lot of time. According to Dr. Bremer's research, it has been proven that tumors are not caused by toxins, as previously believed, but are indeed a microbial disease. Dr. Bremer has also been able to extract these tumor bacteria from the red blood cells of patients, isolate them, and examine their development process. These bacteria are most suitable for a soda-like environment, so it can be known why the elderly are more susceptible to this disease. According to the "acidic basic average" experiment, it is proven that the older the age, the more the average of acidity and alkalinity is affected, because the alkalinity in the blood of the elderly is excessively increased. Although Bremer inoculated the isolated tumor bacteria into the bodies of mice, the mice soon developed obvious tumorous diseases, with sarcomas being the most visible, and true strains can be extracted from these sarcomas. However, after publishing Dr. Bremer's research report, Professor Schilling stated that whether the occurrence of this sarcoma is indeed a tumorous sarcoma still needs to be proven in the future. (National Telegraph, 4th)

(Berlin) Since the shocking news of German bacteriologist Dr. Bremer's discovery of tumor bacteria was released, Bremer published an article this morning stating that he and his assistant Dr. Hamann have cured many people. Dr. Bremer has not only cured early-stage tumors in Berlin and Paris, but also more severe tumor diseases. Dr. Hamann has cured about 60 patients using Dr. Bremer's method. (National Telegraph, 5th)

International Business Telegraph

September 5th, Reuters Special Commercial Report 91

Gold and Silver ▲London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 140 shillings, six and a half pence, down four pence.

London Silver: In the London silver market, selling from China has a dominating influence on the market. The spot price is 21 pence 625, and the futures price is 21 pence 6875, both down 125. After the price drop, the market is stable, with purchases from India and speculators.

Bombay Silver: In the Bombay silver market, although it has fallen by one to three annas, the market situation this morning is still stable. The spot price is 60 rupees, three annas; the September futures are 60 rupees, four annas; and the October futures are 60 rupees, six annas.

Exchange Rates ▲British-American: In the London foreign exchange market this morning, Europe continued to make supplementary purchases. The opening price for British-American exchange was five dollars and two cents, the same as the American-British closing price yesterday. At eleven o'clock, it fell 0625 to five dollars, one cent, nine three seven five, but at noon, it rose 625 to five dollars, two cents, five six two five. At two o'clock in the afternoon, it fell five six two five to five dollars, two cents. Also, one US dollar is equivalent to three shillings, eleven pence, eight zero nine British gold.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs 93, up three pounds. The price gradually rose before noon, and by noon, it had risen sixteen pounds to 75 francs 09. At one o'clock in the afternoon, it fell six pounds to 75 francs 03. This price remained unchanged until two o'clock.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market this morning, the opening price for American-British exchange was five dollars, one cent, eight seven five, down one two five. At ten ten, it fell another one two five. At ten forty, it rose two five to five dollars, two cents. Cotton and Wheat ▲American Cotton: In the New York cotton market, due to the partial failure of the textile industry strike and reports of reduced private cotton production, the opening price rose ten to eleven pounds. After the opening, it fell slightly by two or three pounds, then rose again by one pound. However, at half-past ten, it fell back one or two pounds. The market price at ten forty was either unchanged or up one pound.

Indian Cotton: In the Bombay cotton market today, the price was slightly higher due to buying by speculators. The price of white cotton for the April-May period was 226 rupees, up half a rupee.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market also rose slightly today. At one o'clock in the afternoon, the price for October futures was 6.87, up two pounds.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market trended firmer this morning. At one o'clock in the afternoon, the price for December futures was five shillings, eleven pence, higher than yesterday's closing price by three seven five.

American Wheat: The wheat market opened slightly higher due to signs of reduced grain harvests in Canada and purchases by exporters. Prices were firm before noon. The price at ten forty was up one two five to two five compared to the opening price.

Rubber ▲London: The London rubber market was quiet this morning. At noon, the transaction price for October-December futures was seven pence 625, up 0625 from yesterday's closing price. New York: The rubber market opened firm, with prices up thirteen pounds, expressing sympathy for the London market situation. Prices were unchanged before noon. At ten forty, the price was up one two pounds compared to the opening price.

Securities ▲New York: Before the opening of the New York stock market, the factors favorable to the market were (1) At a time when the situation is uncertain and the recovery of autumn commerce is likely to be delayed, the actions of the securities market can still be considered exciting. (2) Expectations that retail transactions will improve in September. The unfavorable factors for the market are (1) Labor unrest has the most disturbing impact. The current extent of the strike is described differently, but according to recent reports, less than 50% have joined the strike. (2) Steel industry areas have started work after Labor Day, only reaching 22% of normal, a decrease of 4% compared to previous estimates. The market situation was mixed at the opening of the securities market this morning, with prices fluctuating slightly, but there was an upward trend. A slight rebound was expected, but the momentum is still lacking, and it seems that the market will remain sluggish and uninteresting. The New York stock market prices are as follows:

Optimistic Autumn Silkworm Season in Zhejiang Province 93

(Hangzhou) The person in charge of the National Silkworm Improvement Association stated that with the weather improving, the prospects for the autumn silkworm season are now optimistic. Zhejiang Province is expected to harvest 100,000 loads of cocoons. This year, Zhejiang Province is conducting its first trial of autumn silkworm rearing, and plans to conduct large-scale rearing again next autumn. However, current silk prices are extremely low. In addition to Zhejiang Province planning to spin silk and weave silk on its own, the Association is also planning to establish a large-scale Jiangzhe joint silk spinning factory. In the future, it is planned to be jointly operated by officials and merchants, or entirely by merchants, with the government only in a supervisory role. This has not yet been determined and is expected to be established in December or January. (Central News Agency dispatch, 5th)

Dismissal and Investigation of Zhang Zhiyuan, Magistrate of Qingyuan County 94

(Hangzhou) Lu Diping, on the 5th, ordered the dismissal and investigation of Zhang Zhiyuan, magistrate of Qingyuan County, for retreating in the face of danger, resulting in the loss of the city. (Special dispatch, 6th)

Song Ziwen and Yang Hucheng Arrive in Hangzhou 95

(Hangzhou) Song Ziwen arrived in Hangzhou from Shanghai at 8:00 PM on the 5th, residing at Zhou Xiangxian's residence. Yang Hucheng arrived together. (Special dispatch, 6th)

This order.

President Wang Attends Telecommunications Conference and Delivers Instructions 97

Beijing News: The telecommunications conference convened by the Ministry of Communications opened yesterday (the 4th) at 9:00 AM. Those present included Zhu Jiahe, Minister of the Ministry; Zhang Daofan, Vice Minister; Yang Ziyi, Chief Secretary; Wang Fuyi, Counselor; Yan Renguang, Shen Shihua, Gao Tingzi, and Lou Guanglai, Directors; Lu Rongguang, Chief Accountant; Yu Senwen, Director of the Workers' Union; Mao Gongxiang and Chen Dajing, Secretaries; Yin Guoyong, Section Chief of the Telecommunications Department; Huang Renhao, Wen Yuqing, and Yan Gantang, Heads of Local Bureaus; and Chen Shaoxian, Secretary of the Conference, totaling 130 people. President Wang arrived slightly late due to attending a meeting of the Executive Yuan. The meeting was called to order at 9:00 AM with the ringing of a bell. After formalities, Chairman Zhu Jiahe delivered a speech, followed by a speech by Vice Minister Zhang Daofan. Director Yan Ren first reported on the preparations. Subsequently, Advisor Lang Ge, Counselor Wang Fuyi, and Bureau Chiefs Wen Yuqing and Gu Deming delivered speeches in succession. After President Wang arrived, he was immediately requested to deliver instructions and then a photograph was taken. A preparatory meeting was then held, followed by the election of members of various review groups, which were divided into six groups for review. The review meeting continued in the afternoon, and the formal meeting began today. The instructions of President Wang are recorded below.

President Wang's instructions: Chairman, comrades, the Executive Yuan meeting started at eight o'clock this morning and only ended now, so I apologize for my late arrival. Two days ago, a postal conference was held here. On the day the postal conference opened, I came here to say a few words, and I saw many responsible officials from the postal sector gathered together. Today is the telecommunications conference, and I see many responsible officials from the telecommunications sector gathered together. I am very pleased to see this, and I have the same hopes for the telecommunications conference as I did for the postal conference. On the day the postal conference opened a few days ago, I said that since the national crisis, various construction projects have been striving for progress in the face of difficulties, and the most successful ones have been the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Railways. Postal and telecommunications are important state-owned enterprises under the Ministry of Communications, and they have both struggled through various difficulties. Postal services have suffered damage, and telecommunications have suffered the same. Postal services have felt hardship, and telecommunications have felt the same. These two important state-owned enterprises, both under difficult circumstances and suffering great damage, have achieved their current success thanks to the efforts and struggles of Minister Zhu and all the responsible personnel in the face of national crises and other natural and man-made disasters. Telecommunications is a very specialized industry, and I lack that specialized knowledge, so I don't have much to contribute. However, I have a few ordinary and simple words to say to everyone. We all know that telecommunications has not developed much since the Republic. The reason for this lack of development is insufficient economy, and the reason for insufficient economy is poor business. In view of this, the Ministry of Communications is seeking reasonable economic progress and has adopted a cash concentration system. The economic situation of telecommunications now has greatly improved compared to the past, and thanks to the efforts of Minister Zhu and everyone, many other systems have also been improved. The telecommunications industry is a state-owned enterprise; to be precise, it is a state-owned business. However, the telecommunications industry is often subjected to an obstruction and oppression, namely the devastation of military and political organs, which prevents telecommunications from fully developing. I think this must be an important issue to be discussed at the telecommunications conference. I believe that the Ministry of Communications will do its best to find a solution to this problem, and other organs will certainly be able to help. I am willing to cooperate with everyone to the best of my ability so that the opinions contributed by everyone at this conference can be realized. Originally, the telecommunications industry could have been a very prosperous industry, but the reason why it has not been able to fully develop since the Republic is the influence of military and political affairs. In the past, telecommunications had become a form of military warlord separatism, turning the entire industry into fragmented pieces. An industry that could have prospered has become a dilapidated industry, and the future of telecommunications has been greatly affected and hit hard. This is all because the military and political organs do not understand that the telecommunications industry is a business. Secondly, since the invention of radio, a major problem has arisen between wired and wireless telecommunications. We all know that Marconi's invention of radio was a very important contribution to transportation. However, wired and wireless telecommunications seem to have become a state of opposition, as if they are incompatible. In fact, wired and wireless telecommunications each have their own uses and their own positions. As an example, when Special Envoy Huang Musong went to Tibet this time, from Sichuan to Tibet, the entire route was high mountains and ridges, and wired telecommunications were naturally impossible. Because a wireless transceiver was brought along, we were able to communicate news at any time and receive systematic reports. Otherwise, we would not have received any news at this time. Therefore, we can see that wireless telecommunications can make up for the shortcomings of wired telecommunications. However, the situation of wireless telecommunications is now very chaotic. Various provinces and organs are now setting up their own radio stations, and there are also privately set up radio stations in the concessions. We should also find ways to rectify and improve this chaotic system so that both wired and wireless telecommunications can develop systematically. This may also be an important issue to be discussed at this conference. At this telecommunications conference, everyone has put forward many proposals. I believe that after this conference, on the one hand, everyone will contribute their opinions, and on the other hand, everyone will also express the difficulties they have encountered in their work as much as possible. In this way, not only can the Ministry of Communications adopt everyone's opinions and implement them separately, but the difficulties that everyone has encountered can also be resolved. We all know that the biggest difficulty faced by telecommunications is the strong oppression of military and political organs. For example, since the Republic, it has often been seen that the telegrams of important military and political figures are often as long as one or two thousand words, and these one or two thousand words are not important sentences, but elaborate parallel prose. This situation really causes the telegraph operators to suffer a lot. Originally, long telegrams are not necessarily impossible to send, but they must be because it is necessary to explain the ins and outs of a matter and there is no other choice. However, the drafted manuscript should still be revised to make the text as concise as possible. This is not only to take into account the difficulty of telegraph operators sending telegrams, but also especially to save national expenses. I believe that if all military and political organs can think of this, the operating income of telecommunications will be considerable. Moreover, there are two sentences that I often say: First, the nationalization of the army and national defense; second, the commercialization of state-owned enterprises. If the army can become the national armed force and a sharp tool for national defense, then it is a true army. If state-owned enterprises can be commercialized, then they become true productive enterprises. A state-owned enterprise is the lifeblood of the country and the life of the nation, so losses in state-owned enterprises are also losses to the country and the nation. Therefore, these enterprises must be made unified and fully state-owned enterprises, and they must be commercialized. In the future, this type of operation should be done according to the rules of operation. In the past, telecommunications often suffered inexplicable losses. Hard-won construction was destroyed by a sudden storm, causing the responsible authorities to feel disappointed and the enthusiastic staff to feel discouraged. These various disappointments and discouragements will surely be reported as much as possible at this conference. The destruction by military and political organs should make them understand that damage to state-owned enterprises is also damage to their own interests, so they should cooperate fully. The Executive Yuan will certainly do its best to help. Now, I hope that you will speak out about the problems in telecommunications and the external oppression without any concerns. Everyone should speak out about the pain they feel with a spirit of great fearlessness, and reform past mistakes with a spirit of great fearlessness. I hope that everyone will speak out sincerely and that everyone will reform sincerely. (5th)

The New Movement in Nanchang Has Been Effective 98

＝＝The Industry Has Passed the Development and Experimentation Stage＝＝

＝＝And Has Entered the Planning and Implementation Stage＝＝

Nanchang News: The Nanchang New Movement Promotion Association, since being reorganized into the National General Association on July 1st, has progressed from the stage of development, experimentation, and free development to the stage of unified organization, definite planning, and overall forward progress. At this point, the content and effectiveness of the movement's progress here should be something that the general public wants to understand deeply. In order to make all parties understand everything about this and to provide reference, the various situations after the reorganization are described in detail below.

Appointing Instructors from Various Provinces and Cities 99

The General Association was officially established on July 1st, with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek serving as Chairman, and Yang Yongtai, Xiong Shihui, He Yingqin, Huang Fu, Shao Yuanchong, Wu Tiecheng, Chen Guofu, Zhang Xueliang, Yan Xishan, Chen Gongbo, Zhu Jiahe, Shi Ying, Chu Minyi, Yuan Liang, Shen Honglie, Liu Zhenhua, Yu Xuezhong, He Chengjuan, Zhang Qun, Chen Yi, Liu Zhi, Lu Diping, Han Fuqu, He Jian Shao Li, Zi, Song Zheyuan, Xu Yongchang, Long Yun, Liu Xiang, Zhu Shaoliang, Yan Hongkui, Fu Zuoyi, and Wang Jialie were appointed as instructors for various provinces and cities. The General Association has an executive committee under the Chairman, with one Director, one Deputy Director, one Secretary, and one Assistant Secretary, as well as twenty-two executive members. Below are three sections: Investigation, Design, and Promotion. The heads of each section, as well as the Deputy Director, Secretary, and Assistant Secretary, are concurrently held by executive members. Xiong Shihui is the Director, Deng Wenyi is the Deputy Director, Yan Baohang is the Secretary, and Li Huanzhi is the Assistant Secretary. Li Houzheng is the Head of the Investigation Section, Fan Zhengbo is the Head of the Design Section, and Shao Hua is the Head of the Promotion Section. The remaining executive members are mostly concurrently held by military and political leaders.

Nanchang City Work Plan 100

After the General Association was formally established, it informed the New Movement Associations in various provinces and cities to reorganize, and actively planned the promotion work in Nanchang City. The content of the plan includes eight major categories: (1) Measures for government agencies to implement the new lifestyle; (2) Measures for public places to implement the new lifestyle; (3) Measures for stores to implement the new lifestyle; (4) Measures for public utilities to implement the new lifestyle; (5) Measures for city appearance improvement; (6) Measures for factories to implement the new lifestyle; (7) Measures for social organizations to implement the new lifestyle; (8) Preparations for reforming etiquette and customs. The work procedure is that the Investigation Section first investigates various situations and provides the results for the Design Section to use as a reference. Then, the Design Section formulates various implementation measures for the work, which are submitted for approval and then handed over to the Promotion Section for implementation. It is reported that in the past month, the work of each section that has already begun includes "Investigation of Wedding and Funeral Customs in Nanchang City" by the Investigation Section; and the drafting of various measures to implement the new lifestyle movement by the Design Section, divided into the following twenty-three items: (1) Inns and public offices; (2) Teahouses and restaurants; (3) Entertainment venues; (4) Bathhouses; (5) Barber shops; (6) Highways, automobiles, and stations; (7) Vegetable markets; (8) Improvement of public toilets; (9) Rickshaw pullers; (10) Cold food stores and ice shops; (11) Butchers; (12) Tofu shops; (13) Stores; (14) Cleaning of street walls; (15) Street vendors; (16) Docks; (17) Road safety knowledge; (18) General equipment knowledge for social organizations; (19) Training methods for store employees to implement the new lifestyle; (20) Training methods for factory workers to implement the new lifestyle; (21) Training methods for female domestic workers to implement the new lifestyle; (22) Principles for the first phase of the New Movement in various provinces and cities; (23) Principles for the first phase of the New Movement in various counties of Jiangxi. For the Promotion Section, these include convening talks with leaders of various industrial and commercial sectors, and participating in discussion meetings on implementing the new lifestyle in various trade associations and labor unions. Important departments include opening training classes for female domestic workers, guiding the activities of the Youth Service Corps, and deciding that each store should appoint one person as a service member, expanding publicity in the industrial sector, and correcting various ingrained habits.

Achievements in Promoting the New Movement in Nanchang 101

Since the General Association was reorganized and established, the work of the New Movement in Nanchang has shifted from the initial creation and development stage to the planning and implementation stage. Therefore, publicity work has been greatly reduced, such as civic rallies, lantern rallies, and slogan speeches, which are no longer common. The emphasis is now on how to implement and how to execute. Although there has been no precise statistics on the effectiveness of this promotion in the past few months, the following can be observed in daily life: (1) People walking shirtless in the city have disappeared. Previously, a foreigner named Ding Kelan walked shirtless in the street and refused to stop after being warned by the military police, and the authorities have ordered him to leave the country. This is a very significant event. (2) Military police still conduct inspections on the streets, dissuading those who do not fasten their buttons or do not follow the path. The orderliness of the bustling streets is indeed more progressive than before and the situation in major cities. (3) The practice of giving gifts and hosting banquets in various government agencies has decreased. For example, it is stipulated that military and political figures cannot spend more than two yuan on gifts and cannot spend more than five yuan on banquets. Although this is due to the strict prohibition by the highest authorities, it is also the effect of the promotion of the New Life Movement. (4) The practice of large-scale sales and auctions in various stores has decreased, and there are many signs outside saying "Honest price reduction, no false discounts." (5) Hotel and restaurant waiters mostly wear white cloth clothes, know to pay attention to cleanliness, and are more polite than before. (6) The Municipal Council has formulated regulations on patriotic meals for restaurants, stipulating that the highest price cannot exceed ten yuan, and each person uses two pairs of chopsticks and two spoons. Most restaurants comply with these regulations. (7) Young people smoking cigarettes on the streets have disappeared. (8) Barber shops know to use disinfectant, and butchers know to use wire mesh covers. (9) Most public toilets have been improved one after another. Advertising signs and posting signs are all over the city, and the city appearance is very clean. (10) Social gambling has been especially reduced. (September 4th)

Ma Yinchu's Speech in Hankou 102

丨The Silver Problem and Prize Savings丨

Hankou Correspondence: The Hankou Special Municipality Party Affairs Rectification Committee invited Mr. Ma Yinchu, a member of the Legislative Yuan, to give a public speech on the afternoon of the 4th. His speech is as follows:

Prize Savings: "Chairman, distinguished guests, I am very honored to have the opportunity to speak here today. The 11th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society was held in Changsha. Having witnessed the situation in Hunan Province, I feel that there is great hope, but the lack of capital is the biggest problem in Hunan. However, this is the economic problem of the entire China, and it is not only the case in Hunan. Most of China's existing capital is concentrated in the nine major cities of Shanghai, Guangzhou, Tianjin, Hangzhou, Qingdao, Hankou, etc., with Shanghai being the most prominent. Currently, Shanghai has approximately 400 million banknotes, 500 million in silver, and 2.1 billion in deposits. As a result, Shanghai suffers from inflation, while the interior suffers from anemia. Recently, the banking industry in Shanghai, due to the decline of Chinese industry, the bureaucratization and familialization of factory management laws, dares not invest in factories again, and cannot use its capital to engage in speculative businesses such as buying and selling public bonds and land. Because this kind of speculation can only be profitable when gold prices rise and fall sharply. Now that the value of public bonds is stable, this kind of speculation is not feasible. Nor can they use their capital to buy land, because the value of land in Shanghai is declining day by day. Therefore, those with capital are turning their funds to the United States for speculative business. There are now six major companies in Shanghai specializing in this kind of business. Every evening, the lights are bright, the phones are busy, and the business is very prosperous. Last year alone, their total profit reached more than 50 million. However, this kind of speculation is very risky. Today, it is unfortunate that 50 million could be lost. The United States losing 50 million is nothing, but China losing 50 million will plunge its finances into a desperate situation. Moreover, if capital is concentrated in Shanghai, the interior will be empty, and the rural areas will be impoverished. Our country is an import-dependent country and must export silver every year. Therefore, the financial situation in the interior will inevitably become increasingly exhausted. In the event of a second world war, if the enemy threatens Shanghai with its artillery fire and does not allow the use of reserve funds from various bank notes, it will be enough to turn all the banknotes we own into waste paper. If we resist, the economic center of Shanghai can easily be destroyed by artillery fire, causing panic in our rear and making it impossible to maintain. Therefore, the concentration of silver in Shanghai is indeed a great danger. The reason why silver is concentrated in Shanghai is also due to the prize savings of the International Savings Society and the Sino-French Savings Society. This is the biggest reason. As for the prize savings scam to defraud the people's money, that is another secondary issue. The Premier's legacy lies in utilizing foreign capital to develop domestic industry and commerce, while savings societies go against this, using our domestic capital to increase the power of foreign capital, and giving our people's money to foreigners to build foreign houses in the Shanghai concessions. The current savings methods of the International Savings Society are divided into monthly savings of three yuan, six yuan, twelve yuan, etc. The maximum is twelve yuan per month, which must be paid for fourteen years. If one month is not paid, the right to win a prize will be lost, and there is no interest. Paying twelve yuan per month, after fourteen years, no matter which bank you deposit in, you can get 4,831 yuan in principal and interest, while the savings society only gets 2,000 yuan, a difference of more than 2,800 yuan. The savings society uses about 1,000 yuan of this 2,800 yuan as a prize, and the rest is exploited by it. This is one reason. The lottery for prizes by the savings society is held in Shanghai. There is no supervisory organization such as a supervisory committee, and it is difficult for depositors to inquire. What the truth is is ultimately unknown. This is another reason. However, this is still a personal issue. We must consider the future of the entire Chinese economy, oppose the concentration of inland capital in Shanghai, and should disperse Shanghai's funds to the rural areas. If capital flows into the rural areas, the purchasing power of farmers will be strong, urban industry and commerce will develop, and if the rural economy prospers, the enemy's planes and artillery can threaten or destroy a few of our cities, but cannot control our entire rural area. This is the reason why I oppose the prize savings.

The Silver Problem: As for the silver problem, it has a deep relationship with the prize savings and can be combined into a whole problem. Our country uniquely uses the silver standard, while other countries mostly use the gold standard. Since the United States nationalized silver, the price of silver has risen day by day, which has greatly affected us. Before the United States absorbed silver, the ratio of gold to silver was 72 to 1. Now the United States has raised it to 16 to 1. The calculation is as follows: one ounce of silver can be exchanged for one yuan and two jiao nine of paper money, but the casting fee is 50%, so it becomes six mao four fen five of paper money. Half of it is used as its casting fee, but paper money has a market price, and six mao four fen five of paper money is worth six mao nine of gold, that is, one ounce of silver gets three mao nine of gold. As a result, the ratio of gold to silver becomes 51 to 1, that is, one ounce of silver is only worth three mao nine of gold. The formation of this phenomenon has two kinds of causes, near and far, and the near cause can be divided into three, namely (1) The Democratic Party is now in power in the United States. The party has a close relationship with the silver mining capitalists in the United States, so it must raise the price of silver to help its power expand. (2) Prices in the United States have been declining recently, and many factories have closed down, so silver must be used to replace gold, so that the price of gold will fall and prices will rise. (3) The United States wants to increase its exports to our country and compete with Japan's economic power in China, so it raises the price of silver, so that the Chinese can buy more American goods, so that American goods can exclude Japanese goods. As for the distant reasons, there are two. According to my speculation, the United States believes that raising the price of silver will inevitably cause the silver existing in foreign banks to be sold back to the United States. Therefore, China will lack silver, and the countryside will panic. Banknotes must be used to redeem silver, and the remaining silver must be collected. As silver flows out of the country on the one hand, and is collected by people on the other, the result will inevitably be that no silver can be seen at all. The United States then takes the opportunity to lend us silver, just like the previous loan of 100 million silver, to seize the economic lifeline of our country. China has about 200 million silver, and about 50 million exists in Shanghai. According to customs statistics, our silver exports have reached 130 million this year. In the future, after the foreign banks' silver is transported abroad, they will then misappropriate it from Chinese banks. Because of the relationship of import dependency, we have no way to resist, so the Shanghai banking community is short of silver and must misappropriate it from the interior, so that all the silver in the Chinese countryside flows overseas. This is the US policy of raising the price of silver to exclude Japanese goods in China, but I believe that this is impossible. The dumping of Japanese goods in China is not like the previous investment in China. Now Japan exchanges goods for silver, and then sells the silver to the United States to make a profit, and also uses silver to buy raw materials from the United States, such as cotton, which is manufactured in Japan, and then dumps the goods in China, and then sells the silver obtained to the United States, and continues the same buying and selling business. As a result, Japanese goods have not been defeated by American goods, but the United States has been restrained by Japan. The general public in our country has two strategies for rescuing this crisis: (1) Levying silver export tax; (2) Prohibiting silver exports. Those who advocate the former believe that once taxes are levied, silver will not be exported, but I do not think so, because the United States absorbs silver to raise the price of silver, which is a slow process, not a sudden increase in the price of silver. If we levy taxes, the foreign banks' silver will be exported first, and collected in Hong Kong, which is tax-free. When we levy 3%, the silver will be transported to Hong Kong. When we levy taxes to 15%, the silver collected in Hong Kong must be transferred to the United States, and we can earn 12% interest on the silver tax. Therefore, the export tax is useless. As for prohibiting exports, it is also not a solution, because China is an import-dependent country and cannot but export silver. If we buy gold to repay, the price of gold has already risen, and it will not be cost-effective. As for the best way, I believe that the financial authorities should use a clear head, honest administration, concentrate silver, issue banknotes that are not redeemable in law, and pay for foreign goods with banknotes. All necessities of clothing, food, housing, etc., can be replaced by domestic goods. As for the "airplane" and "locomotive" machines in the "travel" aspect, they cannot be purchased with banknotes. Gasoline can be replaced by alcohol. As for clothing, food, and housing, the inflow of foreign goods into China cannot get silver for export, and it is bound to transport our country's products back, and exchange goods for goods. We can not worry about the seriousness of the silver problem. However, this kind of rescue strategy has a close relationship with the prize savings. The US silver policy and the International Savings Society are both economic aggression against us by imperialism. If our country does not ban prize savings, today's International Savings Society will be the second East India Company, and the silver problem will also be unsolvable. I hope that all compatriots and party and government authorities will pay attention to it and urge the government to pay attention to it.

The Dispute over the Wasteland Dam in Wuxi Expands 103

Villagers in Gushan Township, Jiangyin County, crossed the border to demolish the wasteland dam in Chenshu Town, triggering a major dispute. The Construction Department only relied on Engineer Wang's speculative report on water level and hastily approved the opening of the dam. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, considering the high morale of the people in Chenshu Town, could not dissuade them, fearing other changes, telegraphed the Construction Department to send personnel for detailed investigation and to punish Zhou Weisan, the town leader of Gushan. Yesterday's news came, and it turned into an accident. The villagers in Chenshu Town, indignant at the violence of Jiangyin and the deception of the Construction Department, felt that justice was difficult to manifest, so they voluntarily gathered a few days ago and restored the dam to its original state. Unexpectedly, yesterday at about 11:00 am, Gushan Town Leader Zhou Weisan, upon hearing that the dam had been repaired, led hundreds of farmers, carrying farm tools, to the barren dam and demolished the dam without permission, and even wider than before. Workers were also sent to Chenshu Town to cause trouble with hidden iron rulers. All the shops and residents in the town panicked and closed their doors, and the situation was serious, as if Qin and Yue were facing each other. Nearby villagers, upon hearing the news, were filled with injustice and came out to stop them, causing conflicts and fights between the two sides for a long time, and were seriously injured. Chenshu Town Leader Zhou Zihua, upon hearing the news, telegraphed Zhao District Leader to report the conflict and damage situation to County Magistrate Yan for verification. At the same time, Town Leader Zhou felt that the morale of the people was high and he could not dissuade them, deeply feeling that his intelligence was exhausted and he could not cope. Yesterday, he also submitted a report to the county government, requesting reprimand and resigning from his position. County Magistrate Yan has telegraphed the situation to the provincial office for verification.

Liu Luyin Went to Beijing Yesterday 111

After Visiting Wang, He Went to Jiangxi to Visit Jiang

He Expressed His Feelings on the Revival of Germany and Italy

Liu Luyin, the Chinese minister to Italy, returned to China the other day and arrived in Shanghai. At 9:00 am yesterday, he visited Song Ziwen, standing member of the National Economic Commission, Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, and Yang Hu, Director of the Security Office. He returned to his residence in the afternoon and received visiting reporters, and talked about his impressions in Germany and Italy. According to Liu, he has been abroad for almost three years, including two years in Germany and only nine months in Italy. During this period, he deeply felt that the spirit of national revival in Germany and Italy can be used as a reference. He believes that for the revival of a country, the following two points must be paid attention to: (1) The problem of system. Although the systems of various countries are different, they all have their strengths and weaknesses. We may as well take their strengths and abandon their weaknesses to suit the national conditions and use them for adjustment. (2) The problem of people. We can take Italian Prime Minister Mussolini as a model. In my observation, Mussolini's actions are like Zhuge Wuhou in the Three Kingdoms period of our country. His spirit of doing things can be described as "devoting himself to the task until his dying day, indifferent to fame and fortune." No matter how difficult it is, he will move forward bravely, and his governance is especially clear and honest. He is truly a model hero. Therefore, if the whole country can unanimously emulate Mussolini's spirit, then the future of revival can be expected. Liu took the night train to Beijing at 11:00 pm last night to meet with Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, and then went to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Jiang to report on the international situation, stay in Lu for a short time, and then return to his hometown of Wuxue to bury his grandmother.

Domestic Goods Manufacturers Discuss Improving Goods 118

No Crude or Shoddy Manufacturing Allowed

Local domestic goods manufacturers and authorities, in view of this situation, specially convened representatives of more than 30 domestic goods manufacturers at the International Trade Bureau a few days ago to discuss rescue measures. Both Exchanges Set to Merge Starting Next Month 119

The City's Financial Market to Implement Unification

According to the Huadong News Agency, besides the Shanghai Gold Exchange, the city's financial market also has a Merchandise Exchange. Authorities from both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, based on laws and regulations stating that exchanges of the same nature should not coexist in the same location, repeatedly ordered the two exchanges to merge. As such, the merger of the Securities Exchange and the securities section of the Merchandise Exchange was implemented last year. However, the merger of the gold markets was delayed because each exchange held its own ground, and the opinions of both sides were vastly different. Therefore, even after the deadline for the merger set by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry in May of last year, it was still difficult to implement the merger. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry originally intended to enforce it strictly, but due to the mediation efforts of Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, etc., an extension was granted. After this, the merger of the two exchanges was handled by the establishment of a preparatory office, with authorities from both exchanges and Du and Zhang engaging in mutual consultation. After multiple twists and turns, a complete resolution was reached on the 29th of last month. Both sides signed a contract, stating that the gold market of the Merchandise Exchange would be merged into the Shanghai Gold Exchange starting from October 1st. The original capital of the Gold Exchange was 1.5 million, and the Merchandise Exchange would add an additional 300,000, for a total of 1.8 million. In addition, among the original 100 brokers of the Merchandise Exchange, 25 would join the Gold Exchange after the merger. The gold market of the Merchandise Exchange will cease operations by the end of September, and trading for September will end on the 15th of this month, with no rollover allowed. After the merger, the name will remain the Shanghai Gold Exchange, and the location will also be at the original site of the Gold Exchange. None of the directors of the original Merchandise Exchange will join the merged Gold Exchange. After the signing of this contract, the long-delayed exchange merger turmoil was completely resolved. The preparatory office jointly established by the two exchanges at the Great China Hotel has already concluded its work. As for the original site of the Merchandise Exchange at the corner of Sichuan Road and Avenue Edward VII, according to Sheng Pihua, a director of the exchange, they have decided to rebuild it in the near future. The site covers 11 mu of land, and the future use of the site has not yet been determined. It is understood that the original name of the Merchandise Exchange was the Merchandise and Securities Exchange. The initial business included five items: margin trading, securities, cotton cloth, fur, and miscellaneous grains. Among them, the miscellaneous grains and fur items were discontinued shortly after, and the cotton cloth item was also suspended midway due to the Cotton Cloth Exchange. The securities section was merged last year. Now that the gold business has been merged in accordance with the Ministry's order, the exchange is no longer necessary in fact.

Shanghai-Guangdong Chamber of Commerce Discusses Special Tax on Domestic Goods 128

Re-Examination Necessary

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received reports from domestic goods factories in the city that the Guangdong Province was planning to implement a special import tax on goods from other provinces, which would hinder the sale of domestic goods. It repeatedly telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Guangdong Provincial Government and the Guangdong Finance Department, requesting the cancellation of the order. The telegram has been recorded in previous reports. Now it is learned that the Shanghai and Guangdong Chambers of Commerce are discussing the issue of special taxes on domestic goods with each other. The original correspondence is recorded as follows:

Letter from the Guangdong Chamber of Commerce 129

Received your Chamber of Commerce's letter No. 63, stating: "Received a letter from the Enamelware Industry Association on the 9th of this month, stating that according to a letter from members of the Huafeng Enamelware Company, etc., Guangzhou customers claimed that Guangzhou is currently experiencing industrial depression, and major factories and businesses have successively closed. In addition to the original documents on file requesting exemption from redundant narratives, it is proposed that your Chamber of Commerce suggest to the bureau of your province to send personnel to Shanghai before the implementation to investigate and identify which are Chinese factories and which are not, so as to avoid domestic goods manufacturers from being affected equally." Approved this, this case was submitted by the government for discussion, and the case was deliberated and reported back to the government. The suggestion mentioned in the letter from the industry and commerce sectors is a misunderstanding. If your Chamber of Commerce considers it not entirely appropriate, you should make another suggestion to the government so that it is direct. Our Chamber of Commerce will also conduct separate re-examinations to ensure that purely domestic goods manufacturers both inside and outside the province are not harmed and to assist in the process." The letter is enclosed for your reference.

Letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce 130

To the Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce, received your letter No. 874 on the 4th of this month with respect. Shanghai and Guangdong commerce are closely related and cannot be forcibly divided. Your Chamber of Commerce is a fellow traveler and has a duty to help each other. Since it is said that the provincial government's discussion on the special tax case is considered by your Chamber of Commerce to be worthy of re-examination, it is clear that public opinion is in the hearts of the people. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce is grateful to hear this. We urge you to forward the letter previously sent to your Chamber of Commerce to the provincial government and to express your high opinions and thoroughly explain the advantages and disadvantages, so that the authorities will realize that benefiting others is benefiting themselves. Your Chamber of Commerce is close to the water and advocates fairness for the affairs of other provinces with the people of this province, and your position is more likely to be heard than that of our Chamber of Commerce. The success of this case depends on your Chamber of Commerce. As for the suggestion to make a direct suggestion, our Chamber of Commerce has already telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the provincial government since the occurrence of this case. Recently, we received a reply from the provincial government stating that the original telegram has been submitted to the Finance Department for joint review. Yesterday, we also telegraphed the Finance Department to clearly state the advantages and disadvantages. We have heard that your intentions are in line with our intentions and are reporting this together. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce.

Municipal Finance Bureau Takes Over Tax Collection 131

Long-Term Certificates Changed Every Five Years, Tax Amount Reduced

Fees for Collection Procedures Have Been Abolished

The city's brokerage tax has long been designated for education funding and has been handled by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office. The long-term and short-term brokerage taxes in the city area of the old Baoshan County were collected on behalf of the county government by the Management Office. The long-term brokerage taxes in the city area of the old Shanghai County were also collected on behalf of the county government. All short-term brokerage taxes in Shanghai County were handled by merchants on a quota basis. In order to unify administration, the Shanghai Municipal Government submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for approval this spring to take over the city's brokerage tax collection. The Municipal Government then sent personnel to negotiate with the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office to take over the procedures and, following the method of taking over the slaughter tax collection last year, agreed that the Shanghai Municipal Government would allocate 42,000 yuan annually to maintain special education funds. Thus, the city's brokerage tax, which had been collected by the province for many years, was transferred to the city for self-management on the first of this month. Yesterday, the Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice to start the collection. Before taking over, the Finance Bureau, after referring to the opinions of the National Finance Conference on the examination of brokerage tax and adopting the regulations of the Jiangsu Province Brokerage Association, drafted the Shanghai Municipal Brokerage Operation Rules and the Finance Bureau's Detailed Rules for the Collection of Brokerage Tax and submitted them to the Municipal Government for submission to the Ministry of Finance and then to the Executive Yuan for approval and filing. It has also been announced and implemented by the Municipal Government. It is heard that after the Finance Bureau takes over the collection of the city's brokerage tax, the methods have been slightly changed compared to before. The main points are briefly recorded as follows: (1) The registration certificate for long-term brokerage tax was originally stipulated to be 20 years, but now, in order to facilitate the issuance of certificates to merchants, it has been changed to every five years, and the amount of registration tax has been reduced as much as possible (for example, the registration tax for a first-class long-term certificate in prosperous areas should have been 750 yuan, but it has now been changed to 160 yuan). (2) When paying the registration tax, the brokerage firm originally had to pay an additional 10% of the tax amount as a handling fee for the operating expenses of the collection agency. Now that it has been transferred to the city for self-management, the collection is directly collected by the collection offices under the Finance Bureau, and this handling fee is no longer necessary and has been abolished. (3) The items collected with the annual brokerage business tax in the city area in the past included education fees, construction special donations, self-government funds, and collection fees. These have now been abolished. However, the stamp tax that should be affixed to the certificate is still required to be handled in accordance with regulations because it is a central government tax. (4) Article 3 of the Ministry's Measures for the Reorganization of Brokerage Tax, promulgated in June of this year, restricts the commission charged by brokerage firms to 3%. Therefore, the Shanghai Municipal Brokerage Operation Rules promulgated this time also stipulate that the brokerage commission is limited to 3%, which is borne equally by both the buyer and the seller. (5) City area brokerage firms can contact the nearby collection offices to handle the payment of registration tax and business tax. Registration certificates that have not expired must be submitted to the collection office for verification and stamping before the end of this month to remain valid. Certificates that have expired must apply for new certificates in accordance with the regulations. (Regulations omitted)

Anti-Smuggling Association of Cigarettes Held a Meeting Yesterday 132

First Seize Smuggling Operations in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Shandong Provinces

The Anti-Smuggling Assistance Committee for Cigarettes held its first committee meeting at the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance yesterday. Those present were Shen Lishan, Wang Zongzhu, Bao Gengsheng, Chen Shaoqi, Chen Zhongpei, Dong Zhongding, Jiang Yongyi, Jin Gong, Li Xuedong, Chen Maonan, Shen Weiting, Shen Kunshan, Tang Shi, Lao Jingxiu, and others, more than ten people in total. The chairman was Dong Zhongding, and the recorder was He Fangliang. The matters discussed were: (1) First send five teams to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Shandong and other provinces to engage in reconnaissance and seizure. Each team will be led by an inspection commissioner. (2) Take action against tobacco shops and tobacco floss stores, and shall not arbitrarily sell smoked tobacco leaf floss. (3) Households engaged in hand-rolled cigarettes should be registered in the approved areas, and the purchase of tobacco floss must be issued with a purchase permit by the unified tax agency.
