Shanghai Municipal Council Held Board Meeting Yesterday 134

The summer recess of the Shanghai Municipal Council Board has ended, and it reconvened on the afternoon of September 5th. Due to the fact that the Chairman, Mr. Arnold, encountered banditry while traveling through the Northeast on his return to Shanghai from Europe, and also encountered a hurricane in Qingdao, he was unable to return to Shanghai as scheduled, so the Vice Chairman, Mr. MacNaghten, presided over the meeting.

The Chairman announced that Mr. Funatsu, a director, had sent a letter requesting his resignation. Mr. Funatsu has served as a director for six or seven years. His enthusiasm and humble attitude have been unanimously respected. It is a great pity that he is no longer able to serve as a director due to his busy business. After speaking, Mr. Funatsu immediately expressed his gratitude to the directors for their kindness and was especially grateful for the chairman's words. He then nominated Mr. Yamamoto, the Shanghai branch manager of Nippon Yusen Kaisha, as a qualified candidate for the position of director. The directors unanimously decided to publicly elect Mr. Yamamoto to fill the vacancy left by Mr. Funatsu and serve as a director until the end of the current municipal year.

The Rickshaw Management Committee submitted a report to the Board of Directors, stating the work of the committee in August. It stated that since the implementation of the previous agreement, the registration of vehicle owners has continued from August 7th. By the end of the month, only two vehicle owner certificates remained unissued, involving four vehicles.

Chinese and Foreign Charity Association Investigator Reports on Drought Situation in Jiangpu 135

The Chinese and Foreign Charity Association at 97 Renji Road, considering that the drought in various places is extremely serious this time, has sent special investigators to investigate. The report on the drought situation in Jiangpu County is recorded as follows: The terrain of the county stretches from west to east across a large mountain range. The front of the mountain faces the river, and the back of the mountain borders the river. All the fields are divided into two parts: mountain fields and polder fields. The polder fields are further divided into upper and lower polders. The upper polders are no different from the mountain fields, and the lower polders are also difficult to get tidal water due to river siltation. The entire western district is all mountain fields, and the disaster is most severe in this area. The northern district is behind the mountain and is slightly less affected. The southeast district is in front of the mountain and has very few fields, and is even less affected. Since last winter, there has been little rain and snow in the county, and this year it has suffered a severe drought for three months. Statistics show that more than 80% of the county has been affected by the disaster. The crops in the high fields are not to be mentioned, and the drought-resistant grains have also sprouted sparsely after several sowings due to lack of rain. Although there has been autumn rain recently, it is too late to do any good. Food is now causing panic, and disaster victims are begging in groups everywhere. After inspecting for 20 to 30 li, there are no strong men in the fields, and there is no smoke from the chimneys in the villages. Only many disaster-stricken children are seen begging along the way or crying in hunger. It is heartbreaking and tragic beyond description. The county has a charity home, which can house some disaster-stricken children, but the number of people is too large and cannot be accommodated, and the expenses are also difficult, almost unsustainable.

Red Swastika Society Disaster Relief Work 136

Relief for Refugees in Zhenyejiaji

Handling Rice Sales at Par in Eastern Fujian

Investigating the Disaster Situation in Liyang

The Shanghai General Office of the Southeast Main Branch of the World Red Swastika Society received reports from Zhou Genjing, the commissioner of disaster relief in Anhui Province, and the Fuzhou Office regarding the disaster relief situation in great detail. They are recorded as follows: Anhui Luan suffers from severe drought this year, and the disaster is severe. The people are already sighing in despair. Recently, red bandits have continued to appear from time to time in the mountains between Ying and Huo, near the mountain market towns. The people cannot live in peace and have fled with their families, gathering in Zhenyejiaji, Luan. They are emaciated and have no clothes or food. The various tragic scenes are difficult to describe in words. The commissioner was in Luan, witnessed the situation firsthand, and saw the tragedy and could not help but file a petition on their behalf. After hearing the report from Commissioner Zhou, it was immediately discussed and telegraphed back to Commissioner Zhou, approving the allocation of 2,500 yuan from the relief funds to relieve the refugees in the Zhenyejiaji shelter.

The Fuzhou Office telegraphed that the 2,000 shi of rice allocated by the society was shipped to Fuzhou, but it was appropriately timed to when Fujian Province was not peaceful, and upstream traffic was blocked, so it could not be transported separately. Now that traffic has gradually resumed, transportation is still difficult. It is now found that the disaster area in the five counties under the jurisdiction of Funing in Eastern Fujian is in dire need of rice after the robbery. 500 shi of rice has been allocated and handed over to Chairman Lin Baoqi, together with Jun Hu, to escort and transport it for rice sales at par. It is heard that the office has telegraphed back to follow the instructions.

The office has paid close attention to the drought in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces and has determined that Liyang County in Jiangsu Province is the most severely affected area. Chairman Li Cikai of the office personally went to investigate and found that a family of eight had committed suicide by closing their doors. The tragedy that occurred in the northwest several years ago has now been staged in the southeast. It is hoped that people in the southeastern provinces will not ignore the disaster just because it has not yet reached them.

Citizens Should Pay Attention to Diphtheria, Meningitis, and Other Diseases 137

Health Bureau Has Established Preventive Vaccination Centers

Injections by Various Offices, Hospitals, Etc.

As summer ends and autumn arrives, seasonal epidemics will again become prevalent. In order to prevent them, the Municipal Health Bureau has decided to divide the city into 50 prevention centers starting from the 15th of this month to administer vaccinations to citizens. The details are as follows:

Summer Cholera Has Passed Peacefully 138

According to You Jihua, the director of the South City Office of the Health Bureau, cholera and smallpox, which were prevalent in the summer, have been eliminated since autumn arrived. This year, due to the effective prevention by both the Chinese and foreign concessions, only two people contracted cholera, which can be said to have passed peacefully. The places with the highest incidence of cholera and smallpox internationally are Calcutta, Marmagoa, and Mathes. There is a possibility of occurrence in these places regardless of whether it is winter or summer. From the 18th to the 31st of last month, 143 people contracted cholera and seven people contracted smallpox.

Diphtheria and Meningitis Will Occur 139

Now it is autumn again, and the most prevalent seasonal epidemic diseases are diphtheria and meningitis. These two diseases can become prevalent on cloudy days with low air pressure and on dry days with high air pressure. Children under the age of five should take preventive measures the most. Diphtheria should be prevented by injecting toxin antitoxin needles in advance. In order to avoid accidents for two or three years, it is hoped that middle and upper-class citizens will not hesitate to spend a yuan or two on the needle fees. As for the meningitis vaccine injection, the bureau can provide it free of charge.

More Than Fifty Free Injection Sites 140

The Health Bureau believes that the absence of diseases among citizens is the happiness of the entire city. Therefore, it is making every effort to prevent seasonal epidemics. The epidemic prevention office for preventing cholera and other diseases this year will be closed. The bureau will start preventive vaccinations on the 15th of this month, dividing the sites into fifty locations. Various health offices, hospitals, and registered qualified doctors will provide free vaccinations and administer vaccinations.

Local Court Announces Schedule for Burning Confiscated Drugs 141

Lou Ying, the chief prosecutor of the Shanghai Local Court, issued an announcement yesterday, stating that the list of items related to opium cases that should be burned for the three months from April to June of the 23rd year of the Republic of China has been prepared. According to the Jiangsu High Court Chief Prosecutor's Order No. 1077, the burning will take place at 1:00 PM on September 10th of this year. The burning will be held in public at the open space next to the rear of the court at the time specified above. In addition to sending letters to various agencies to send personnel to supervise the burning on the due date, the names of the opium offenders, the date of acceptance of the case, and the amount of drugs and the number of opium paraphernalia are announced in advance so that the public can know. The total includes 32,782 red pills, 19 catties, 21 taels and 8 qian, 123 taels and 5 qian and 8 fen, and 1 catty of opium, 9 taels and 7 qian of opium paste, 192 opium bubbles, 1 tael and 5 qian and 6 fen of morphine, 20 taels and 8 qian, 59 small packages, each package containing a small amount of opium paraphernalia and ash, etc., totaling 7,832 pieces, and the number of unopened packages stating the amount is not counted, and if multiple pieces are combined into one piece in the unopened package, it is counted as one piece, from large pieces like a package of opium pills to small pieces like a small amount of opium bubbles, all are counted as one piece. (Names of opium offenders omitted)

Railway Electrical Signal Expert Yang Ke Returns After Completing Studies 142

Yang Ke, courtesy name Yanming, an electrical engineer, is the second son of Mr. Yang Qianli, Tianji. He graduated from Jiaotong University in 1930. Afterwards, he worked at the signal office of the Beining Railway for more than a year. In January 1932, he went to study in the UK, interned at the British Power Railway Signal Co., and participated in the signal installation projects of the Metropolitan Railway, London North Eastern Railway, and London Midland and Scottish Railway. After completing his internship, he returned to China and arrived in Shanghai on the Italian ship Conte Rosso the day before yesterday. It is heard that Mr. Yang will go to Beijing soon to continue working in the Ministry of Railways.

Destitute on the Shores of Shanghai with No Food or Accommodation

An Aging Woman with a Fondness for Adornment, Mrs. Qin Zhan, Encounters Robbers Early in the Morning 148

A Robber Fires a Shot and a Stray Bullet Wounds a Passerby

Qin Yushan from Hubei Province works as a recruiter for major hotels and ocean liners, and lives at No. 356 Fuyou Road in the city. His monthly income is reasonably adequate. Qin's wife, Zhan, although aging, has a fondness for adornment. Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, as usual, she carried a basket to the market to buy vegetables. Unexpectedly, upon returning home, just as she arrived at the entrance of Mingzhu Lane on Fuyou Road, two robbers wearing dark-colored shirts and pants suddenly jumped out from the roadside. One robber pointed a gun at her side, forbidding her from making any noise, and immediately snatched a gold bracelet from her. They carried it and fled south. However, Zhan, seeing her gold object being robbed, shouted loudly to catch the robbers. One robber, in desperation, turned around and fired a shot. A stray bullet hit Zhang Jinxiang, a Hangzhou native who collects paper scraps and cinders, in the right leg. Zhang fell to the ground in pain. Wei Kun, a policeman from the No. 6 post of the First Sub-District of the Second District, upon hearing the alarm, rushed to the scene and bravely gave chase. However, at that time, there were many passersby near the City God Temple, and the policeman was unable to fire his gun. Therefore, the two robbers took advantage of this opportunity and quickly disappeared into the crowd. Afterwards, Chief Shen Zhenhua led the police to the scene and sent the injured person to Shanghai Hospital by car. He also reported to the Inspectorate by phone.

A Female Student Narrowly Escapes Abduction 149

Realizing She Was Being Abducted Midway

Police Officers Find the Abductor Flees

Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, Lu Zixiang, from the 39th post of the Sixth District at the intersection of Baihe South Road and Yidingpan Road in Western Shanghai, was on duty when he suddenly saw a girl with a beautiful face, short hair, wearing a cheongsam, and carrying a schoolbag, about ten years old, standing still and crying beside the post. He immediately went forward to inquire, but the girl cried even more sadly and did not answer a word, as if she were lost there. He immediately took the girl back to the Sixth District. After interrogation by District Officer Xing, the girl stated her name was Qin Baodi, twelve years old, and she lived at No. 83, Anlan Lane, Xuejia浜 in the South City. This morning, she left home to go to school. Because it was still early, she held two small yuan and wanted to buy a pen at a certain tobacco and paper shop. Just as she was knocking on the door of the shop, an unfamiliar man suddenly came from behind and told me to go with him to buy it. I believed him to be true and followed him for many roads, to near Jing'an Temple. I realized that I was being abducted and firmly refused to go. He forcibly dragged me to near the police post. Because my legs were weak and I could no longer walk, I stood and cried, intending to report it in the meantime, but I dared not speak. The man mistook my intent to report and immediately ran away. Seeing that I had escaped from the tiger's mouth, I was panicking when I was spotted by the police officer. District Officer Xing, after hearing her statement, determined that the girl had been abducted but had fortunately escaped by a clever plan. He immediately sent her to the bureau for disposal.

The China Merchants Bureau's Pu'an special express steamer, which used to operate the Putuo special route, has been discontinued. Starting from the 8th of this month, it will regularly travel the Shanghai-Qingdao route, with the following scheduled sailing dates: Every Saturday at 9:00 AM, it departs from Shanghai and arrives in Qingdao at 2:00 PM on Sunday. Every Tuesday at 9:00 AM, it departs from Qingdao and arrives in Shanghai at 3:00 PM on Wednesday. The ship docks at Pier No. 1 of Qingdao's Dà Gǎng port and the China Merchants Wharf in Pudong, Shanghai.

The Slaughterhouse Company's Two Factions of Workers Involve in Armed Fight Case Concluded 151

Two factions of butchers from the French Concession Slaughterhouse Company in Pudong and Jiangyin engaged in a fight last month. Xu Zhongqiu, Yao Shengxiang, Xu Mingde, Wu Fuda, and Ren Jintang, five people from the Jiangyin faction, were injured by knives and axes. The patrolmen arrived and arrested Qin Haichang, Gao Shanyun, Wang Renren from the Pudong faction. Subsequently, Chen Jinhai and four others from Pudong, suspected of instigating the fight, were arrested and transferred to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. After the interrogation, the case was postponed for further investigation. It was reported in the previous news. Yesterday, Judge Zhang Chaozuo continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. First, the victim Ren Jinbao testified that at 12:00 midnight that night, he and four companions went to work at the company and were stopped by Chen Jinhai, who held a pistol to them and forbade them from working, forcing them into a dark alley. He saw more than twenty people who, without asking any questions, attacked them with iron rods and axes. He was slashed in the back by "Ā Sì Má Zi" (possibly a nickname) and fell to the ground screaming for help. He only recognized Chen Jinhai and their associates, as well as the people they had called in from other gangs. Based on this, the court interrogated Chen Jinhai, who categorically denied being at the scene, claiming that he was innocent and framed because his associates had reported them. Asked, "What does the associates' fight have to do with your boss?" He replied, "They suspect that I called the associates to report them." The court then summoned the defendant Chen Jinhai's witness, Gu Qiusheng (who had appeared in court last time), who testified that Chen Jinhai came to my place that night, as agreed the night before, to talk, and then he went back alone. At this point, Chen interjected, "Wasn't there a dog walker who came to call me at that time?" Gu also said that a dog walker had come, but he did not know his name. After questioning, the judge ordered the start of the debate, which was conducted by the patrol's lawyer Fei Xizhen and the two lawyers hired by the defendant, Wang Shizong and Jiang Yiping. After the lawyers debated the attached private prosecution, the court announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict for ten days later. The defendants were returned to custody. Chen Jinhai also filed a petition for bail, which the court ordered to be granted upon payment of a 3,000 yuan bond and a 3,000 yuan shop guarantee.

Family Members Request Transfer to Hospital for Treatment

Page 14

President of Tongde Medical College, Dr. Gu Yuqi, Encounters Danger 153

A Patient's Family Transforms into Extortionists

Forcing Gu at Gunpoint to Write a Note to Take Money Home

The Rickshaw Puller's Heroic Action of Jumping out of the Window to Save His Master is Laudable

Gu Also Jumps from the Window, Suffering Multiple Injuries

Dr. Gu Yuqi, the current president of Tongde Medical College at the intersection of Tongfu Road and Dagu Road, is originally from Wuxi. Because of his deep knowledge of medicine, he is highly trusted by patients. Earlier this month, a patient named Zhang requested a house call. This person lives in a three-story attic in a Westerner's house at No. 228 Huanlong Road. This was the third time this patient had requested Gu to provide treatment. Yesterday, after being invited by the patient, Gu went to Huanlong Road in his own car around 1:00 PM. Gu had a rickshaw puller as his attendant, to carry his leather bag and do other work. As usual, he accompanied Gu into the room. As Gu was taking the patient's pulse, several members of the Zhang family stood by. Unexpectedly, one of these people suddenly took out a pistol and struck the rickshaw puller on the head with the gun butt. The rickshaw puller immediately broke his skin and bled, falling unconscious for a moment. At the same time, another person among the group took out a gun and pointed it at Gu, demanding that he hand over his money immediately. Gu said that he had no money on him, and that his checks and other valuables were not with him, and that he needed to go home to get them, and told them that everything could be discussed. The other party immediately ordered Gu to write a note. The tone of the note roughly said, "The rickshaw puller's life is in danger, quickly go home and get money to redeem him." The note was written as if it were written by Gu's rickshaw puller. While Gu was writing the note, the rickshaw puller who had fainted woke up and saw his master in trouble. He disregarded his own safety and jumped out of the window on the third floor. Unexpectedly, because he was too high off the ground, he was injured on the spot in the lane there. Nearby neighbors gathered when they saw this situation. The people in the room, seeing that their plan had been exposed, scattered and left. Before leaving, they ordered Gu to wait ten minutes before coming out. At this time, Gu, fearing further danger, dared not go out through the front door, and also jumped out of the window. Because there happened to be a bed placed on the ground there, intending to jump on the bed, he failed to land properly and also fell to the ground. Neighbors who saw this gathered even more. At this time, Gu's rickshaw puller waited for a long time and did not see Gu come out, and there was noise from the back door. He left the rickshaw to investigate and saw this situation. He ran madly to Gu's friend's place, borrowed a telephone, and reported to the police and called for an ambulance. The Xuehuali Road patrol station dispatched a detective and an ambulance to send the two injured people to Guangci Hospital. The rickshaw puller's injuries were minor, but Dr. Gu suffered multiple injuries.

The Exchange Rate of Silver Dollars Plummets 154

The exchange rate of silver dollars for copper coins in this city had previously reached 3,360 copper coins per silver dollar. It has gradually declined over the past month, but has remained around 3,300 copper coins. Unexpectedly, starting the day before yesterday, it plummeted to 3,240 copper coins. Yesterday, the market rate even fell to 3,180 copper coins, meaning each silver dollar was exchanged for 3,180 copper coins. It has plummeted by more than 100 copper coins in two days. The exchange rate of silver dollars for silver dimes has also declined. Yesterday, each silver dollar was exchanged for 302 dimes.

Ten Thousand Pieces of Japanese Kelp Arrive Yesterday 155

The Largest Batch Since January 28th

Since the January 28th Incident, large quantities of Japanese kelp vegetables have not been shipped to Shanghai. Although some were shipped later, they were only three or four hundred pieces. Recently, Japanese marine products have been sold at low prices in various ports in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Therefore, yesterday, 10,000 pieces of kelp were shipped from Otaru and Yokohama in Japan, which is one of the largest batches of Japanese kelp imported since the January 28th Incident. It has been unloaded into the Huishan Wharf warehouse and will be completely transferred to various ports along the Yangtze River.

Panic over the Impending Closure of Private Postal Services at the End of the Year 156

Sending a Letter to the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association for Assistance

Submitting a Petition to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for a Five-Year Extension

The Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai received a letter yesterday from Hua Yunjin and others, representatives of the private postal services, requesting assistance. The original letter stated: "Greetings. According to the private postal service representatives Hua Yunjin, Wang Wenjiang, Wang Tongren, Wu Yunyu, Ren Shiting, and Yin Wutong, etc., our industry has been ordered by the Ministry of Communications to cease operations by the end of this year. We are extremely anxious that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Inland Chambers of Commerce have repeatedly appealed on our behalf, but have not received approval from the competent authorities. Most of the people in our industry are fellow townsmen from Ningbo and Shaoxing. Now that the deadline is approaching, the lives of tens of thousands of fellow townsmen are at stake, and we must explain it clearly to your association. Private postal services have a history of over a hundred years, and they exist in both large cities and remote rural villages, involving countless connections. Can closing them down be completed in a few months? This is the first point. Most of the employees in various places are old and frail laborers, totaling no less than 30,000 to 40,000 people. Their livelihoods are at stake, which is an urgent and critical issue. Once unemployed, they will inevitably become starving corpses. This is the second point. Recently, industry and commerce have been declining throughout the country, and this year's drought is especially unprecedented in nearly a hundred years. The people in our industry cover agriculture, industry, and commerce, and are all in despair at this dead end. Is it possible for the country to disregard the lives of the people for the sake of postal unification, and is the Premier's Principle of People's Livelihood suitable? This is the third point. Various chambers of commerce and public institutions in various places have a strong need for private postal services, so they have consistently maintained them. This is a clear fact. Ordinary small industrial and commercial people have a particularly close relationship with them due to the convenience of delivery. The fellow townsmen from Ningbo and Shaoxing are even more of an exception, receiving assistance due to their proximity. This is the fourth point. In short, national policies and the lives of the people must be considered together in order to maintain fairness and reason. Therefore, the only solution now is to set a five-year deadline, with our industry issuing a written guarantee to gradually close down, which can alleviate its difficulties. The country has been operating the post office for forty years, and the effect of unification can be achieved in the near future. At this critical juncture, we have no choice but to risk offending and respectfully request your association to consider the feelings of our hometown and the urgency of our situation, to present the situation to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Committee, to create blessings for our fellow townsmen, and to graciously order the Ministry of Communications to extend the deadline for five years to allow for closure. Then, our hometown will be grateful and our families will be blessed. We humbly submit our words of gratitude and await your instructions. Respectfully presented to the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai." (Below omitted)

The Hotel Industry Opposes Increasing Police Rates, Supplementing Three Reasons 157

Yesterday, a petition was again submitted to the Municipal Council

The Xinsheng News Agency stated that the hotel industry has repeatedly opposed the Municipal Council's increase in police rates. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the industry again sent representatives Sun Qiuping, Chen Wenda, Gu Jiemei, Zhang Renliang, Zhang Qiyuan, Li Jiemei, Liu Qirun, Zhan Wenxi, Yao Hongchu, Zou Jincheng, etc., to petition the Municipal Council's Director He Dequi, supplementing the points not detailed in the past as follows: (1) The Ratepayers Department has repeatedly stated that if any of the businesses that have been added to the rates consider the increase unreasonable, they can apply to the Assessment Committee for reassessment. However, the Assessment Committee is not a third party, but merely an agency attached to the Municipal Council. To request the Municipal Council to reassess the rates that the Municipal Council has increased in order to seek exemption from the rates is like seeking the skin from a tiger. This is why the representatives are unwilling to apply to the Assessment Committee for reassessment. (2) The Taxpayers' Meeting resolved that, without the authorization of the taxpayers, no arbitrary increases in rates shall be made, except for newly built houses and rented city houses. Now, the Ratepayers Department has had a fanciful idea, using the prices of hotel rooms as a tool for assessing and increasing rates. However, the businesses that have been added to the rates had already been assessed by the Municipal Council in the past. Now, there is a sudden change in practice, is this not a contradiction in itself? And where does this place the resolution of the Taxpayers' Meeting? (3) Since the January 28th Shanghai War, there have been countless Japanese and Westerners who have defaulted on rates and taxes. The Ratepayers Department does not focus on this when rectifying tax collection, but disregards everything and imposes exorbitant taxes on our hotel industry, fully demonstrating the Ratepayers Department's weakness of bullying the kind and fearing the fierce. Our hotel industry is in a precarious situation, and we are forced to embrace a great determination and vow to persevere to the end. If the Ratepayers Department consistently refuses to accommodate us and withdraws its decision, we will not hesitate to make any sacrifices or be softened by any threats (i.e., revocation of licenses). Director He promised to submit the matter to the Board Meeting for discussion, and the representatives were satisfied and dispersed.

The French Concession Strictly Cracks Down on Rabid Dogs 159

Dog Owners and All Sectors Should Pay Attention

The Health Department of the Shanghai French Concession Municipal Council, after finding that cases of rabid dogs biting people have occurred recently within the concession, has already presented the matter to the Superintendent-General Fu Lesi and decided to strictly crack down on them. In addition to notifying all dog owners, it will also distribute notices on preventing rabies. The notices are copied below: (1) Notice Regarding the Crackdown: It has come to our attention that there have been multiple cases of rabies in the French Concession recently. Strict measures have been adopted to suppress the spread of infection. Dog owners must strictly comply with Article 1 of the Bureau's regulations on dogs on the road. Any dog found walking on the road without a muzzle will be arrested by the patrolmen, imprisoned in the dog pound. In addition, dog owners must have their dogs vaccinated against rabies. This is the notice. (2) Notice Regarding Precautions: It has come to our attention that there have been multiple cases of rabies in the French Concession recently, and several people have been bitten by rabid dogs. Residents within the concession should pay attention to the following points: (1) What is rabies? Rabies is a severe disease. Although this disease is not contagious, humans can contract it by being bitten by a rabid animal. (2) Method of transmission: Whether this rabies is transmitted from animal to animal or from animal to human, the method of transmission is through bites, scratches by cats, or being licked on a wound by a rabid animal. The more wounds there are, the greater the risk of contracting rabies. The farther the wound is from the central nervous system, the less severe the rabies. Bites to the face are the most dangerous, followed by bites to the hands, upper body, and lower body, with the severity of rabies decreasing as the bite location descends. (3) Several symptoms of rabies in dogs: When a dog first contracts rabies, its temperament suddenly changes, gradually becoming melancholic, depressed, suspicious, and silent. It will avoid solitary and dark places, and its guarding ability will gradually decrease. If someone calls it, it must be forced to obey. It will crawl, with its ears drooping, and stare at its owner with a gloomy gaze. At this time, the dog has no intention of biting. Its appearance still appears healthy, and sometimes its appetite even increases. However, these symptoms increase rapidly, and the dog's suspicion becomes increasingly severe, often hiding in dark places, suddenly standing up, then suddenly lying down, repeating several times and constantly fidgeting. The disease then becomes more severe, leading to paralysis or madness. Therefore, if there is any change in a dog's habits or appearance, it should be suspected of having rabies and sent to a veterinarian for examination. (4) Methods of preventing rabies in dogs: A veterinarian can vaccinate a dog against rabies, providing immunity for approximately one year. (5) Consult a doctor immediately and do not delay.

City Police Bureau Detective Team Breaks Private Arms Cache 161

Two Handguns Seized From Four Suspects

Confessed to Trafficking; Handed Over to Bureau for Legal Action

City Police Bureau Detective Team Deputy Leader Dong Wenrui received a tip that bandits were transporting firearms from the French Concession to the Xieqiao area in the Chinese district, intending to commit robbery. Dong immediately reported this to Detective Team Leader Lu Ying, who promptly dispatched several armed detectives, along with police detectives from the Second District, to Xieqiao around 8 PM the previous night. They lay in ambush on all sides. At 10:30 PM, two bandits approached in the darkness. The officers shouted "Catch them!" and surrounded them, apprehending Xie Hongsheng from Yancheng and Lü Delin from Ningbo. A five-inch Browning handgun with ten bullets was found on Xie. They were taken into custody. Lü confessed that another handgun was hidden at the home of accomplice Xu Zijie from Shaoxing, located at 213 Lujiazhai, Hutai Road, near the Sun Temple in Zhabei, at 204 Tianbao Lane, Haining Road, Zhabei. Acting on this information, the officers escorted the suspects, along with the Zhabei police, to the address, apprehended Xu, and confirmed the existence of another handgun, which had been sold to accomplice Yang Wenqing from Baoshan, residing at 27 Changxing Road, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. Officer Lu dispatched the same officers yesterday morning to the aforementioned location, where they apprehended Yang and confiscated a handgun with seven bullets. They were taken into custody. Yang confessed that he was currently working as a cook for Jardine Matheson & Co. and was also a member of the Pengpu Defense Corps. He stated that the handgun was purchased on behalf of a relative, Shui Ayang, and that he entrusted Xu Amao, a member of the Second Regiment of the Defense Corps in Lujiazhai, to buy it for thirty yuan, sixteen of which had been paid on the first of this month. Fearing accidents, he had Xie Hongsheng transport it. Officer Lu, considering the case involved the transport and private possession of firearms, ordered the four suspects, along with the two handguns and seventeen bullets, to be handed over to the Third Section of the General Bureau for legal proceedings.

Robbers Posed as Passengers and Robbed the Bus South of Caohejing

Two Police Officers Fought Bravely Against Four Robbers, Killing One; the Rest Escaped

The Shanghai-Pinghu intercity bus operated by the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Long-Distance Bus Company on Guohuo Road in the Nanshi district, Bus No. 6, which departed from Shanghai at 10 AM the previous morning, was robbed of cash, foreign currency, and jewelry worth over a thousand yuan from passengers Liu Cui and others near the railway south of Caohejing Station. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Further details are as follows: At 10 AM the previous morning, Shanghai-Pinghu Bus No. 4196, carrying over twenty male and female passengers, was driven by driver Zhang Lansheng to the Tushanwan Station. Two robbers, one wearing a white short shirt and pants, and the other wearing a dark raw silk long gown and a straw hat with a pockmarked face,

Posing as Passengers 165

purchased tickets to Qianliangmiao Station. At 10:20 AM, about two miles south of Caohejing Station (i.e., north of the Huiling Station railway), the two robbers who boarded at Tushanwan revealed their sinister faces. Each drew a handgun, first forcing driver Zhang Lansheng to stop the bus, and then robbing passengers Liu Cui and three others. The items stolen included: (1) From female passenger Liu Cui, who lived next to the church in Haiyan, a jade bracelet, a jade ring, a diamond platinum watch, a gold ring, a small leather wallet, a Bing Chu gold pocket watch with a gold chain, two jade pendants, and a gold cigarette holder and gold toothpick, plus over ten yuan in cash; (2) From Wang Jiahou, who lived on Tinglin West Street, a gold watch; (3) From Tao Taiqing, who lived on Minhang North Street, a gold ring and nineteen yuan in cash; (4) From Huang Xingji, who lived on Shi Street in Pinghu, a check for three hundred yuan and over ten yuan in cash.

Total Losses 166

were estimated to be over a thousand yuan. At that moment, driver Pan Liansheng, driving a bus from Minhang to Shanghai for the same company, passed by. Zhang Lansheng signaled the robbery. Upon learning of the situation, Pan Liansheng sped to Caohejing Station and telephoned the Sixth District Third Precinct of the Municipal Police Bureau. Precinct Chief Wu Zhengding, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched patrol officers Yuan Desheng, Li Huapu, Fu Guohui, Ma Jilong, and others, leading a team of officers, and rushed to the scene to encircle and apprehend the robbers. He also notified the Meilong outposts of the Longhua harbor by telephone. At the same time, the two robbers on the bus, seeing the bus from Minhang to Shanghai pass by, dared not rob any further. They demanded the keys from driver Zhang Lansheng, opened the door, and fled to the northwest.

Fled in Panic 167

By the time the officers arrived, the robbers were already far away. They split up to track and pursue them. At Huacun Temple, passing the Sanguantang and turning north to Baziqiao (an area under the jurisdiction of the Hongqiao Township outpost of the First Precinct of the Sixth District), they spotted two men who resembled the robbers walking ahead. At that time, only police officers Deng Zhenxiang and Li Shuangying were present; the others had scattered. The two robbers noticed them and immediately opened fire to resist arrest. Deng and Li also drew their guns and returned fire. Seeing that the situation was not favorable, the robbers crossed several rivers. Pursuing them to the Puhuitang River, the robbers swam to escape. Deng and Li bravely crossed the river to continue the pursuit. At Wangjia Lane, east of Hongqiao Township, two robbers suddenly jumped out from a thicket of branches and willows beside a house, each drawing a handgun and joining the fierce battle. Gunshots rang out, and bullets flew like rain.

Both Sides Clashed 168

The battle lasted fifteen minutes, with a total of sixty or seventy shots fired. One of the two robbers was shot by Officer Deng in the left chest and fell in front of the ancestral hall east of Wangjia Lane. He was apprehended, and a six-inch Browning handgun, No. 129012, was seized. Another robber was shot in the left foot and was carried away by the two robbers who had been lying in ambush. Officers Deng and Li, being over ten miles from their station and running out of ammunition and reinforcements, did not dare to pursue them further. Dying from Injuries 169

The robber was about thirty years old, with a flat-top haircut, wearing a white silk short shirt over a white undershirt, white cotton pants, dark brown silk socks, and black satin-topped leather shoes. Later, Prosecutor Tang from the District Court, accompanied by an examiner, arrived to conduct an autopsy. Woman Commits Suicide After Suffering Mental Breakdown Following Husband's Death 171

Wang Bao, a woman from Ningbo, aged 41, resided at 133 Datong Road, Zhabei, in a three-story attic room. Her husband, Wang Zhaowei, died of illness on December 27th of last year. Since then, she had been living alone and supporting herself by running a fruit stall in the vicinity. In March of this year, Wang Bao gave birth to a posthumous daughter. Due to a lack of breast milk, she sent the infant back to her ancestral home to be raised. The day before yesterday, at noon, Wang Bao's nephew, Wang Ziyu (who lived on the second floor), called her for lunch but received no response. He went up to the attic and found her lying on the floor, covered in urine and feces, with a hemp rope around her neck. Alarmed, he cried for help. Neighbors gathered and discovered that she had hanged herself with a thin hemp rope. Due to her obesity, the rope had broken. Despite attempts to rescue her, it was too late. Yesterday morning, the local Fifth District Third Precinct instructed the local guard Li A'er to report the incident to the District Court for an autopsy. Subsequently, Wang Ziyu, 24 years old, from Ningbo, and currently working as a craftsman at the American Electric Material Company, claimed to the court that the deceased, Wang Bao, was his aunt. Since his uncle's death, she had suffered a significant mental shock, often expressing a desire to end her life and attempting suicide, but had been persuaded to return home. This time, unfortunately, she succeeded. He also stated that her mother's family was still in her ancestral home and had already been notified. They would arrive in a few days. Fearing future complications, he reported the incident to request an autopsy and offered to arrange for the coffin and funeral. Subsequently, Prosecutor Lei Binzhang, accompanied by an examiner, arrived at the scene and confirmed the facts, instructing that a coffin be prepared and further instructions awaited.

Achievements of Traditional Chinese Medicine Practitioner Gu Baiyan 175

Traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Gu Baiyan is known for his profound medical knowledge and extensive experience. He is particularly skilled in treating lung disease with hemoptysis, liver and stomach ailments, neurasthenia, kidney deficiency with spermatorrhea, prenatal and postpartum conditions, and menstrual irregularities due to blood deficiency. He is also quite adept at pediatric medicine. Last month, the eldest son of Mr. Fang Maohua, an employee of this newspaper, fell ill with a high fever all over his body, which worsened at night, causing restlessness and delirious speech, excessive thirst and urination, and extreme irritability. He was treated by renowned pediatricians and repeatedly by massage experts for over twenty days, all to no avail. The child, only three years old, became increasingly weak, and his condition deteriorated daily. Mr. Fang was extremely anxious. Subsequently, according to friends, Gu Baiyan, a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner at 46 Heng'an Lane, Nanyang Bridge, outside the West Gate of this city, possessed medical ethics and skills unlike ordinary doctors, meticulously diagnosing illnesses and carefully prescribing medication. Seeing his son's worsening condition, Mr. Fang consulted him. Unexpectedly, after three doses, the fever gradually subsided; after six doses, the facial flushing disappeared; and after eight doses, the excessive thirst and urination stopped. He is now completely recovered. This illness was a case of latent heat. If not treated properly, it would have developed into consumption, threatening his life. Fortunately, he encountered a good doctor like Gu, who was able to bring him back to health from a serious illness.

Xinmin News Agency Sends Letter Requesting Xinmin Telegraph Agency to Change Name 177

The Xinmin News Agency was founded eight years ago and has been registered with the Shanghai Municipal Party Department. The current president is Cheng Xingzhi, and the reporter is Mr. Min Lianqin. Although the scale is relatively small, its contribution to the news industry is not insignificant. Recently, the agency read in the newspaper that Mr. Tang was planning to establish the Xinmin Telegraph Agency, scheduled to begin operations on September 1st. The agency immediately had its legal counsel, Mr. Yu Xiangqin, send a letter to the telegraph agency, requesting that it change the name "Xinmin" to avoid confusion. Because newspapers often abbreviate news sources to "Mou Mou She" (lit. So-and-So Agency), without distinguishing between "Tongxun" (news) and "Dianxun" (telegraph), the first two characters are crucial and must not be the same. This is obvious. Since Mr. Tang is also working hard for the news industry, he should also share the same enthusiasm for protecting the long-standing Xinmin News Agency and immediately change the name of his telegraph agency.

August Report on Benevolent Deeds of the Universal Goodness Villa 181

Since its establishment over twenty years ago, the Universal Goodness Villa has consistently undertaken benevolent deeds such as burying the exposed and providing medical treatment, which are genuinely significant in relation to public health. However, it has always lacked designated funds and relies entirely on the enthusiastic assistance of philanthropists from all walks of life. Reading Q&A

The Issue of Self-Study for Women After Marriage Continued 188

丨丨 Answer to Wang Yuqi 丨丨

Mr. Wang raised a question about women's self-study, asking why married women are unwilling to study. Today, we will first present the primary reason for women's decline after marriage, which is the lack of social economic status, in response to Mr. Wang's question. When the manuscript was being copied that day, the clerk made a mistake and wrote Liu Xunyue instead of Wang Yuqi. This is hereby clarified. Editor

On the positive side, women cannot find the use of knowledge in society. On the negative side, they are burdened by household affairs. Household affairs are the chains that bind all women, and the greatest subjective cause of eroding women's desire for knowledge. Many people believe that women are physiologically inferior to men, but this is not the reality. Women's inferiority to men is due to the iron chains of household affairs placed around their necks. After the trap of "men managing external affairs and women managing internal affairs" has been set, it has become impossible. With the burden of household affairs, women become slaves to the family, slaves to men, and household puppets with no possible activities other than bearing and raising children and serving their husbands. This kind of bondage firmly holds women, whether in the old Chinese joint family or in the fashionable one-husband-one-wife new family. For example, in a new-style family, can women not bear children? Can they not raise children? Even if laundry and cooking can be hired out to maids, the task of directing and managing those so-called household chores still falls to the housewife herself, not to the man. Even if we step back and say that all household affairs can be delegated, because of the burden of household affairs and the fact that family values, under the support of tradition, cannot be shaken off for a time, the relationship between men and women cannot but be built on the family, with the family as the only goal for men and women to pursue together, and with the family as the bond of love between men and women after marriage. If the family breaks up, everything is over between men and women! In this way, neither men nor women are willing to disrupt the peace of the family unless absolutely necessary. As the housewife, the woman is forced to let her neck be chained within this yoke, even just for eating and sleeping.

If women are to become members of society, they must step out of the narrow confines of the family and attend to the world at the same time. We believe that the relationship between women and men should be a combination of sincere love, and this love should be built on mutual aid, mutual understanding, and efforts in social undertakings. In this way, women become completely free people, completely independent people, and, like men, can only seek their survival in academics and careers. May I ask, what things that men can do cannot they do? Why would they not work hard to acquire advanced knowledge as a weapon for survival?

In China, the family system naturally has many more drawbacks than in Europe and the United States, and a virtuous wife and good mother have always been regarded as divinely ordained. Women not only cannot become members of society, but even the little bit of rights they previously fought for, such as going to school and public socializing, are now in danger of being lost. This phenomenon can be seen everywhere at present. It is naturally not uncommon for people like Mr. Liu's friend to give books on social science to his woman to read, and for another person to hope that his woman can study literature with him, but this is definitely not the general situation. Many young gentlemen are afraid that their wives will show their faces in public and enter society, and even before they can complete their studies, they sever all their contact with society.

Therefore, the fact that women do not seek to improve themselves after marriage cannot simply be blamed on women's own depravity, but there are major objective reasons for this. If we want to solve the issue of women's self-study after marriage, we must start by fundamentally resolving the contradictions between their living environment and their thoughts.

As mentioned above, establishing women's social status and independent economic rights, as well as liberating them from household affairs, is the primary meaning of women's liberation. It is the main condition for women to be able to obtain true equality and freedom in their careers and studies. However, this is related to the entire social reform problem and cannot be achieved with a single move. Here, it can only serve as a goal for people who are concerned about women's liberation and women's self-study issues to strive for.

Therefore, what we can talk about is only how to make their lives conducive to the conditions for self-study. (To be continued)

Special Article

Reducing Railway Freight Rates and Developing the Rural Economy Wu Shao Zeng 190

Considering that the current railway freight rates for agricultural products are high, those of the second class such as lychees, longans, raw silk, etc; those of the relatively low fourth class such as various fruits (except for a portion with special prices) and Lingbao cotton, Shaanxi cotton, etc; and those of the lowest fifth class such as rice, wheat, grains (except for a portion with special prices) and Tongzhou cotton, Taicang cotton, Hankou cotton, Jiangxi cotton, etc. In general, the method of determining freight rates is based on the distance of the journey, with higher rates for shorter distances. The longer the mileage, the lower the freight rate per ton per kilometer. Those transported on this line all adopt the principle of decreasing distance. Those transported by joint transport of each lines, there are even percentage rates of decreasing distance for joint transport freight rates, that is, after five hundred and one kilometers, a reduction of one percent is collected according to the fixed amount, and from then on, for every one hundred kilometers, a reduction of one percent is collected, up to a full journey exceeding two thousand five hundred kilometers to reduce collection by twenty percent, And the so-called joint transport freight rate is the total amount of freight calculated by each line. Considering the reasons, it is nothing more than taking care of the transportation costs of each line. Therefore, the freight rates of each line have not been able to be unified, and all agricultural products related to the rural economy, except for those included in special prices, can only be calculated according to the fixed rate to calculate the freight. This situation, at first glance, seems to be fair, but upon closer inspection, it is not enough to be reasonable, (1) For the same goods traveling a distance of 500 kilometers, if transported jointly by Lines A and B, the freight rate per ton is 20 silver yuan. If transported jointly by Lines B and C, due to the different transportation costs of Lines A and C, it may increase to 30 silver yuan per ton. Using the same goods traveling the same mileage, and shouldering freight rates that differ greatly, how can it be said to be level, (To be continued)

Weather Report 191

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that there were thunderstorms in several locations around Shandong, with winds varying from northwest to northeast. In the middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the surrounding area, the wind came from the northeast to the east. Around Taiwan and in the southern East China Sea, the weather was poor and there was a strong cyclone, caused by a hurricane in the Bashi Channel moving northwest by north. The center of the hurricane, at 2:00 PM, had advanced to within 60 miles of the intersection of 23 degrees north latitude and 121 degrees east longitude, with fierce winds. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the local temperature in this city reached a high of 85.1 and a low of 71.6. On the same day last year, the high was 86.7 and the low was 67.1.

Order from the Ministry of Education Regarding Equipment Standards for Junior High School Botany and Zoology (1) 200

On the 4th, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of each province and city, stating that the equipment standards for botany and zoology in junior high schools, and biology in senior high schools, have been formulated by the Ministry. In addition to being announced by ministerial order, twenty copies of these standards are being sent to be forwarded to all subordinate middle schools for compliance. This order.

Equipment Standards for Junior High School Botany and Zoology 201

▲ Contents

(1) Names of Student Experiments, (1) Junior High School Zoology, (2) Junior High School Botany, (2) Equipment, (1) Instruments (2) Live Animals and Plants, (3) Specimens, (4) Charts, (5) Models, (6) Reagents, (7) Glassware, (8) Other Supplies.

Explanation 202

(1) These equipment standards were formulated by the Curriculum and Equipment Standards Compilation Committee of the Ministry of Education based on or with reference to the following materials: (1) The junior high school zoology and botany curriculum standards and the senior high school biology curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry; (2) The opinions of various authors; (3) The opinions of domestic biologists and botanists; (4) The opinions of domestic middle school biology teachers and botany and zoology teachers.

(2) These standards are divided into the following seven types. The first three types are permanent equipment, and the last four types are temporary materials that need to be added annually. (1) Instruments, (2) Preserved Specimens, (3) Charts or Models, (4) Live Specimens, (5) Reagents, (6) Glassware, (7) Other Supplies.

(3) These standards list thirty-two senior high school biology student experiments to comply with the Ministry-promulgated curriculum standards of one experiment per week.

(4) Sixteen student experiments are listed for each of junior high school botany and zoology.

(5) The various botany, zoology, and biology equipment listed in these standards are determined as the quantities required for selecting experiments for one class of students. As for the number of students in a class, it is divided into four groups of five students each, with twenty students as the standard.

(6) These standards propose both ordinary and minimum quantities.

(7) The quantity of reagents is determined based on the convenience of purchase, so it is slightly more than actually needed.

(8) When demonstrating, models are more realistic than charts, but the price of models is more than ten times higher than charts. If schools have financial difficulties, they can use charts.

(9) In addition to common live specimens, efforts should be made to cultivate them in the laboratory or nearby, and display them at all times for observation.

(10) The preserved specimens listed in these standards are the minimum teaching equipment. Schools should add other specimens as much as possible according to local conditions.

(1) Names of Student Experiments in Junior High School Zoology

(1) Study of Rabbit Adaptation and Habits, (2) Characteristics of the External Structure of Birds, (3) Understanding the Life of Six Kinds of Wild Birds in Multiple Seasons, (4) The Life History of Chickens, (5) Live Goldfish and Their Food, (6) The Life of Frogs and Toads, (7) The Life History of Frogs, (8) Estimation of the Number of Earthworms in the Garden, (9) The Life of Snails, (10) Silverfish, Mantises, Ant Colonies, Wasps, Moths, Butterflies, Water Striders, (11) Insect Rearing Methods, (12) Insect Collection, (13) Flies and Their Prevention and Control, (14) Mosquitoes and Their Prevention and Control, (15) Spiders and Their Living Habits, (16) Internal Parasites of the Human Body.

(2) Names of Student Experiments in Junior High School Botany

Establishment of the Business Management Design Committee of the China Vocational Education Society 203

(Shanghai Society) The Business Management Design Committee, initiated and organized by the China Vocational Education Society, held its inaugural meeting and first regular meeting at the Society yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. The details are as follows:

▲ Attending Committee Members: Huang Renzhi, Xu Changqing, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Qin Hancai, Yao Zhongliang, He Qingru, Yao Huiquan, Jia Foru, Wang Yinfo, Wen Chonglu, Shi Yangyong, Yang Chonggao, Huang Zhuming. Chairman Jiang Wenyu, Recorder Shi Yangyong.

▲ Business Management: First, Huang Renzhi expressed specific opinions on business management, saying that he has recently become most interested in scientific management. In the past, various organizations rarely paid attention to business affairs. It should be known that the scope of business affairs is the largest and the relationship is the most important. For example, documentation, accounting, and general affairs all belong to the business aspect. Currently, there are special books for the study of documentation and accounting, and special lectures, but the general affairs aspect is uniquely lacking. There is a real need for research and training. The training steps should first determine the methods and then start training talents. It is hoped to create a well-defined path that ordinary people can rely on and learn from. In his personal opinion, the solution to this problem has the following points: (1) Determine the target, such as schools, factories, and administrative agencies, and discuss them separately. (2) Determine the scope, such as specifically referring to general affairs. (3) Analyze the parts, such as procurement management, workers, storage of goods, internal and external cleanliness, meeting arrangements, food handling, house repairs, and temporary events such as fire, sudden illness, and theft. (4) Specify the steps, such as procurement requiring the opening of the product name, explaining the purpose, the required date, after approval, using what method (either bidding or purchasing), drawing a formal invoice, etc. (5) Provide various major forms or documents, such as procurement procedures, storage ledgers, management of workers' essentials, handling emergency alarms, etc. If the methods can be studied in detail and concrete methods can be obtained, then it will not be difficult to further seek talent training.

Discussion of Proposals: After Huang's presentation of specific opinions, Xu Changqing, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, He Qingru, and others successively expressed their opinions. At the end, the proposals were discussed: (1) Proposal to nominate members to organize the opinions of the committee members, decided to nominate Huang Renzhi, He Qingru, Xu Changqing, Jia Foru, and Shi Yangyong to take charge. (2) Proposal for the date of the next meeting, decided to hold it at 3:00 PM this Saturday. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Special Article

The Issue of Civic Education in National Revival (4) Zhang Yuangruo 210

Speaking again of "rites", Westerners are polite everywhere. For example, when walking on the road, if they bump into someone, foreigners do not care whether you bump me, or I bump you. They are all very polite and say sorry. If Chinese people bump into someone, they will start scolding and fighting, without any manners. At the same time, when foreigners buy things, they do not rush to be first, but go in one by one in order, just like primary school students lining up in a neat team. These are all manifestations of their rites, and also the reason why their society is orderly. Finally, speaking of "trust", the Westerners' spirit of keeping promises can best be shown at banquets. Chinese people are very different. Even if they are invited to dinner at six o'clock, they will not start until ten o'clock. Because the Western countries have these four virtues, their people can be loving and united. In other words, the reason why their nations can unite is that the four things of benevolence, righteousness, rites, and trust are used to unite them. However, these four virtues are the inherent doctrines of our country. In recent years, although there have been constant calls for unity in China, we are still unable to unite today. This is because the social morality of benevolence, righteousness, rites, and trust, which is inherent in our country, has not been promoted. Looking back at the social morality of benevolence, righteousness, rites, and trust in Western countries, it has developed so well, so they can unite, can work hard, and sacrifice for the country, for the nation, for society, and for others. Therefore, their nations can generate strength and create the wealth and strength of their nations. How should we reflect deeply?

Third, the spirit of diligence of the people. The people of Western countries are generally very diligent and thrifty. You must not think that Western material civilization is so developed, so you want to consume and enjoy it. You must know that the true meaning of material civilization is to create material, use material, not to enjoy material, and waste material. Chinese people generally only know how to enjoy and waste material, but do not create and use material. They are really criminals of material civilization. Western material civilization is so developed, but their people's spirit of hard work, thrift, cherishing material resources, and creating material is far beyond what we can reach. This is not the source of their wealth and strength. I have never been willing to praise Western nations, but this spirit is indeed worthy of admiration. They sit in a bright and brilliant environment, but are generally very diligent and thrifty, more diligent and thrifty than we are in suffering and hardship. When I was in Belgium, I saw the living conditions of their people. The life of a middle-class family is quite difficult. Breakfast is just a few slices of bread and a cup of coffee. Lunch is just one or two dishes. The evening is as simple as breakfast, but they are very diligent in doing things. They get up at dawn and do not use servants. All rough and fine work is done by themselves. In the period of national crisis, the general people, especially the people in the cities, still do not know how to strive, and still do not get up until the sun is high. They live together all day long, without mentioning righteousness, indulging in consumption, and not engaging in proper business. Some even advocate the strange theories of "dancing to save the country" and "entertainment to save the country". How can we seek the revival of the nation? I hope that the authorities will make practical corrections to this kind of decadence.

Secondly, speaking of the situation of the Japanese nation, the development of the Japanese nation also has three reasons. Although these three reasons are not exactly the same as those of Europe and the United States, they are also similar.

First, "Japanese Obsession" - The Japanese people's national consciousness is like hypnosis, as if they are obsessed. So it is called "Japanese Obsession". This can be divided into three points:

(1) Believing in the Country. They say that the Great Japanese Empire is created by gods, and is an unparalleled Great Empire that stands tall in the world.

(2) Believing in the Nation. They say that the Japanese nation is chosen for them by gods. The Japanese nation is the most outstanding nation in the world, so they desperately protect their nation, even if they are clearly wrong, they still desperately fight with others.

(3) Believing in the Imperial Lineage. The slogan of the Japanese Restoration is to respect the emperor and expel the barbarians. They believe that their Emperor is the only ruler in the world, and everyone absolutely supports him.

Because of this "Japanese Obsession", the Japanese nation produced the above three results, and his nation therefore generated an undeniable power.

Second, Bushido. Bushido is the driving force of the Japanese Restoration movement. Its spirit is a struggle for life, a struggle for the survival of the nation and the country. Because of this spirit of struggle, they produced their "life of blood and tears". Blood is the spirit of bloodshed and sacrifice for their monarch and the nation. Tears are the spirit of loving and caring for their people. The Japanese people, living in this kind of struggle for life and life of blood and tears, are therefore dictatorial internally and able to resist externally. This is the second reason why the Japanese nation is strong.

Third, Passionate Emotions. There are also three spirits expressed from the Japanese people's passionate emotions:

(1) The Genuineness of Faith. The Japanese nation's faith is very firm, which is the Japanese obsession I just said, as if they were hypnotized.

(2) Struggling for the Greater Self. Being able to sacrifice the lesser self to struggle for the greater self.

(3) Not Planning. This is also a good thing about the Japanese nation. Chinese people always consider and plan for their personal interests first when they encounter something. If there is something unfavorable to themselves, they refuse to do it. As for asking them to struggle and sacrifice for the country and the nation, that is even more impossible. But the Japanese are different. They never plan for themselves, and are willing to take responsibility and sacrifice bravely. We remember that during the Russo-Japanese War, they encountered a river that they could not cross. They never planned and scrambled to fill the river, allowing their troops to cross it. They not only did not retreat, but also thought it was more glorious to be buried underneath. This shows the Japanese people's spirit of not planning, being responsible, and sacrificing bravely.

The Japanese have a sincere faith, so they can not plan. Because they do not plan, they can be very responsible and bravely struggle and sacrifice for the greater self. The Japanese nation, because its people have this kind of passionate emotion, generates passionate power. This is the third reason why the Japanese nation is strong.

Fourth, the main principles of civic education in our country in the future. Now I have roughly spoken about the causes of the rise and fall of various nations in ancient and modern times, both Chinese and foreign. From these many objective and obvious longitudinal historical traces and horizontal world affairs, we can summarize the important principles that should be paid attention to in the future civic education of our country. I do not admit that these principles are any new theories. They can only be regarded as platitudes. Do not think that platitudes are bad. You must know that the most valuable things in the world are platitudes. Platitudes are just like everyday meals. We eat three meals a day. Have we ever gotten tired of eating them? In our natural physiology, we cannot take strange things as our daily food. Similarly, in the physiology of society, we cannot use strange theories to treat the masses as experimental animals. Fine wine is beautiful, but it can hurt the body. Heretical sayings can mislead people and ruin the country. Therefore, those who are truly hygienic will never be greedy for pleasure. Those who can truly serve the country with loyalty will never sing high-sounding tunes. Based on this belief, I believe that the main principles of civic education in our country in the future should be based on the following three points:

First, enlightening national consciousness. To enlighten national consciousness, I think we should at least follow the following points as creeds:

Page 17

Shen Bao Domestic Goods Weekly

A Few Words of Contribution

Three Small Gifts to仰葊 215

— 仰葊

▲Dedicated to the Leaders of Domestic Goods Factories

When considering the current state of domestic goods, there are countless complexities, but the key points are simply these three:

(1) How to reduce costs? For the same product, why do others make money while we lose money? For the same piece of yarn, why can others make money selling it for 160 yuan, while we lose money selling it for 180 yuan? For the same bolt of cloth, we always lose money selling it for three yuan, while others profit selling it for two yuan? Sometimes, even drinking ginger soup to warm our stomachs, we say they have government subsidies, but in reality, there is no such thing. We constantly say they are dumping and selling at low prices, but no one in the world does business at a loss. They are willing to sell cheaply because they have their own clever methods. First, cheaper raw materials; second, sophisticated and well-maintained machinery; third, reduced labor; fourth, dedicated work; and fifth, no embezzlement by administrators. Government assistance means convenient transportation and thorough protection. Banker assistance means low interest rates. Academic assistance means in-depth research and significant contributions. With efforts from all sides, results will naturally follow. This is the first key.

(2) How to improve products? For the same product, why do others innovate, constantly changing patterns and coming up with new designs, making good things even better and refined things even more refined, while we remain the same? Naturally, we will either not advance or regress. Ordinary people always like novelty. If, for the sake of promoting domestic goods, we insist on forcing people to use old-fashioned items, it is not reasonable. Therefore, factory products should follow the principle of "If one day is new, then make it new again, truly every day new," as stated in the Great Learning, to defeat foreigners and maintain stable profits. Otherwise, if we only promote domestic goods verbally, it will eventually become annoying. To improve products, first, recruit specialized technicians; second, pay attention to production machinery; and third, have excellent designs, constant research, and continuous observation and investigation to seek continuous improvement. Is it really impossible to catch up with others?

(3) How to increase production? For the same factory, others can manufacture quickly and produce in large quantities. Our common problem is that we often fail to deliver goods on time. When sales are brisk, we have no goods to sell. By the time we have more goods, the season has passed. How can we calculate the losses in this situation? I visited Kangyuan, Wuhe, and other factories the other day. Their manufacturing is calculated with extreme accuracy. When to start the machine, when to deliver the goods, with only a few minutes of difference. Know that with the same capital, the same workers, the same machines, and the same expenses, how much difference is there between fast and slow? This all depends on strict organization, planning, clear rewards and punishments, and accurate auditing. From the organizers to the junior staff and trainees, they must have undergone scientific training and have a scientific mindset.

Talks on Domestic Goods

Silver Exports and Domestic Goods 216

— Ding Xing

Since January of this year, China has successively experienced large-scale silver exports. Economists have written articles discussing the advantages and disadvantages. We ignorant small citizens, of course, cannot understand the profoundness. Even if we have any good contributions, we cannot get the adoption of the great gentlemen!

However, since the 21st of last month, there have been consecutive large-scale silver exports, with workers rushing to make silver boxes overnight and carrying them away in a hurry... all kinds of news have been published. It is said that "the total amount is 100 million yuan."

The Shen Bao's editorial on August 26th said in the last paragraph: "...Let's take a look at how abundant the silver that Shanghai Chinese banks have collected from the interior in recent years is, and how it shows the concentration of funds. Then look at the state of urban and rural areas. I'm afraid no one will have a satisfactory conclusion! If this is the case, even if silver never flows out and is piled up in the vaults, can our national economy make any progress?" Indeed, in the eyes of us who do not understand economics, silver exports certainly have considerable benefits. Otherwise, would the smart banking community do such a stupid thing?

The Shen Bao on August 26th: "Imports of perfume and cosmetics in seven months exceeded 1 million yuan." The same day's Xinwen Bao: "Imports of cigarettes in six months approached 20 million yuan." The same source: "Trade deficit with Japan in July reached more than 2.9 million yuan." ... Such shocking news, is this huge amount not "silver exports"? It's just flowing out secretly, unknown to the Chinese people.

The United States' raising of silver prices and buying of silver was originally for the sake of preparing for war, while China's silver exports are for profit. However, the biggest key is that the large-scale silver exports reduce the value of foreign goods calculated at gold prices, so a large number of foreign goods are added to the Chinese market out of thin air, and dreamy Chinese people will flock to them. I believe that in the current critical time, it is even more appropriate for everyone to be of one mind and truly "use domestic goods." It must be understood that the invisible export of silver is just buying foreign goods and sending money overseas, which is more harmful than the tangible export of silver.

Everyone understands very well that silver exports are closely related to the rural economy. At a time when provinces across the country are experiencing floods and droughts, there are also large-scale silver exports. Isn't this an extremely contradictory thing? That is why I have explained "tangible" and "intangible." Tangible may still be profitable; intangible, however, is like flowing water, gone forever, without any benefit, and becoming less and less, drier and drier, until it is completely extinct. At that time, it will be truly "helpless."

"Truly using domestic goods" and "persuading friends and relatives to use domestic goods" are the most important and supreme personal matters for Chinese people to address "to others" and "to oneself" now!

Discussion on Domestic Goods

Competition and Squeezing 217

— Quan Jia

Within the domestic goods industry, we can often hear about mutual competition. This is not bad news, as long as competitors do not intend to squeeze each other out, competition can make products better. In other words, competition will advance the domestic goods industry. However, some large-capital merchants, in order to dominate their industry, disregard profits and losses and squeeze out small-capital businesses, making it impossible for them to stand. This is a crisis for the domestic goods industry.

For example, Factory A makes a bolt of cloth, and Factory B also makes a bolt of cloth. If Factory A and Factory B compete, then Factory A will try to research how to prevent the cloth from fading? Factory B will also find a way to make the cloth less likely to tear? Isn't this very beneficial? Because the best way to improve an object in the world is through competition.

What if there is squeezing? Because Factory A has more capital, it doesn't care about losing money and reduces prices to compete, so others have to lower prices too. Eventually, Factory B has no choice but to close down. What about Factory A? It doesn't care about the quality of the cloth and the reputation of others, so buyers of domestic goods have to buy foreign goods or even completely lose faith in domestic goods. This is very important!

The above has been said in detail. Below, I want to tell the wise buyers:

(1) If there are two items, both of which are domestic goods, you should choose the one with a higher price and better quality. Second, you should write a letter to the store with the inferior product, telling them to improve their product and advising them to work hard to improve.

(2) If you have research on the manufacture of goods, that's even better. You should provide specific improvement methods for the reasons why the product is impractical or of poor quality, and give them to the manufacturer for reference. Or tell them the advantages of foreign manufacturing and tell them to improve.

I think that national factories all want to improve their products, and there will be a valuable competition in an intangible way. Isn't this interesting? However, having the ambition to dominate the market is bound to fail!

New News from the Domestic Goods Industry in a Week

(1) The Ministry of Industry has notified the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce that the request to prioritize the use of domestically produced building materials has been communicated to all regions for compliance.

(4) The United States needs domestically produced asbestos, and France needs copper magnets, jade, Xiang embroidery, and various art products. Those who wish to promote sales overseas can contact the International Trade Bureau.

(5) The International Trade Bureau's statistics for the total value of shark fin imports in the first seven months of this year is 1,791,653 yuan.

(6) The Shanghai Women's National Goods Year Movement Committee has appointed Ms. Lin Kecong to lead the publicity for using domestic goods in other cities.

(7) The China National Manufacturers Joint Conference has decided to send personnel to various factories to investigate organizational equipment.

(8) The China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association has invited Mr. Xiang Kangyuan to report on his impressions of the Nanyang investigation.

(9) The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent another telegram to the Guangdong Department of Finance regarding the Guangdong Provincial Government's levy of special taxes on domestic goods, requesting that it be cancelled as soon as possible.

(10) The Shanghai Mechanized Domestic Goods Factories Joint Association, together with the Industrial and Commercial Management Association, has jointly established a factory management training institute.
